**MFD navigation is via the always-present HEADER, NOT an "INIT hub" — KEEP the page picker (#105).** Investigated the theory that "every MFD page is reachable from INIT" (true-ish on the A320/A330 MCDU via the physical page keys): it is **FALSE for the A380**. Source (`FmsHeader.tsx`) shows every FMS page carries a persistent header of 4 dropdown tabs — **ACTIVE** (F-PLN/PERF/FUEL&LOAD/WIND/INIT), **POSITION** (MONITOR/REPORT/NAVAIDS/IRS/GNSS/TIME), **SEC INDEX** (SEC 1/2/3), **DATA** (STATUS/WAYPOINT/NAVAID/ROUTE/AIRPORT/PRINTER) — plus the top system tabs (FMS/ATCCOM/SURV/FCU BKUP). INIT is just one item under ACTIVE; it has no links to other pages. **Sighted pilots navigate via this header, not through INIT.** Crucially, the MFD scrape does NOT capture the header tabs (verified live: 0 header-tab elements scraped though 40 `_MFD_pageSelector` DOM nodes exist — they're the navigateById click targets, outside the scraped content area), so the **"Go to MFD page" combo is currently the ONLY way a blind pilot can reach most pages** (besides the quick buttons + Ctrl+arrows). It is the accessible equivalent of the always-visible header — strictly better than expanding 4 dropdowns one item at a time. **Do NOT remove the page picker** — it would strand the user. (Confirmed: keep it.)

**ATC COM / CPDLC + D-ATIS — navigate by UIService URI, NOT page-selector id.** The page-selector ids (`{CAPT|FO}_MFD_pageSelector{Tab}_{idx}`) only exist while that *system's* header is mounted, so the FMS-header `navigateById` click can't reach ATCCOM from an FMS page. The reliable cross-system path is the MFD's own **UIService.navigateTo(uri)** — verified live to jump from `fms/data/status` straight to `atccom/msg-record`. The UIService isn't always on `fsInstrument` directly; `A.mfdUiService()` resolves it from `document.querySelector('a380x-mfd').fsInstrument.uiService` OR `…mfdCaptRef/mfdFoRef.instance.uiService` (the mounted side). `A.navigateUri(uri)` (agent) → `navigate_uri` command (`CoherentDebuggerClient`) → `SendNavigateUri` (`FBWA380MCDUForm`). The six ATCCOM pages are in `AllPages` with a non-empty `Uri` field (page-selector dispatch picks `navigate_uri` when `Uri` is set, else `navigate_by_id`); the **ATC COM button** (Alt+A) now fires `SendNavigateUri("atccom/connect")` instead of the old KCCU-only `navigate_by_id("",-1,"ATCCOM")`. URIs (from `AtccomHeader.tsx`): `atccom/connect`, `atccom/request`, `atccom/report-modify/position`, `atccom/msg-record`, `atccom/d-atis/list`, `atccom/emer`. **Live-verified all 6 navigate + scrape as clean DOM text:** CONNECT (NOTIFY TO ATC / ACTIVE+NEXT ATC / DISCONNECT ALL / ADS-C toggles), MSG RECORD (the CPDLC log — ALL MSG / MONITORED MSG, where uplinked clearance text reads when `A32NX_DCDU_ATC_MSG_WAITING` fires), and D-ATIS (DEP/ARR + UPDATE/PRINT) are functional; REQUEST / REPORT & NOTIFY / EMER read "ERROR 404 NOT FOUND" — **WIP in the FBW dev build**, not our bug (will surface once FBW implements them; MSFSBA already navigates to them). The MSG RECORD page being empty with no datalink connection is correct (no CPDLC messages = nothing to read). This is the read path that complements the existing "ATC Message Waiting" auto-announce, which only flagged a message but couldn't read its content.

**SEC (secondary) flight plan reading.** The SEC pages read fully via the normal scrape — the agent + `buildFplnLines` treat them identically to the active plan (clickable waypoints + discontinuities included). URIs (from `MfdPageDirectory.tsx` / `utils.ts`): SEC INDEX = `fms/sec/index`; per-plan = `fms/sec{1|2|3}/{f-pln|init|perf|fuel-load}`. `AllPages` now reaches SEC via the UIService URI path: **SEC INDEX** (`fms/sec/index`) + **SEC 1/2/3: F-PLN** (`fms/sec{n}/f-pln`); the **SEC FPL** quick button (Alt+P in the MCDU — Alt+S is the scratchpad jump; stale "Alt+S" claim fixed in the 2026-06-12 docs audit) navigates to `fms/sec/index`. The SEC INDEX page itself exposes F-PLN/PERF/INIT/WIND/FUEL&LOAD as buttons, so the rest of each secondary is reachable from there. (Replaced the old `SecIndex` page-selector-id entries, which only worked while the FMS header was mounted.)

**BTV predicted landing distance + rudder-trim readouts.** (1) The BTV **predicted** landing distances for the selected runway — dry, wet, estimated stop point — are read in the OANS window (MAP DATA tab) and the panels (the standalone `FBWA380NavDisplayForm` ND window was REMOVED — see the SUPERSEDED display-windows note), from `A32NX_OANS_BTV_{DRY,WET}_DISTANCE_ESTIMATED` / `_STOP_BAR_DISTANCE_ESTIMATED`, which are **plain metres** L-vars (NOT ARINC429, unlike the in-rollout `REMAINING_DIST_TO_EXIT/RWY_END` words). Shown in metres + feet; the "not being computed" gate keys on dry/wet only (stop-bar carries a constant ~40 m front-of-aircraft offset even at rest — verified live: dry/wet 0, stop-bar 40 on the ground). (2) Rudder trim ("weather trim") in the Flight Control Computers panel now reads `A32NX_SEC_1_RUDDER_ACTUAL_POSITION` — the ARINC429 degrees word the PFD/SD show (positive = nose-**Left**), decoded in `TryGetDisplayOverride` to "Left/Right X.X degrees" / "Neutral" / "Not available" — instead of the stock `RUDDER TRIM PCT`, which does not track the FBW SEC-computed trim.

**EFB Failures page — already accessible via the flyPad WebView2 scrape (no code needed).** The flyPad EFB's **Failures** app is reachable from the EFB nav (Shift+T → "Failures" link) through the existing `coherent-flypad-agent` scrape + WebView2 browse view. Verified live: the landing page lists the ATA-chapter categories (ATA 21 Air Conditioning … ATA 46 Information Systems) as links plus a Comfort/Compact view toggle and a Search box; drilling into a chapter (e.g. ATA 24 Electrical Power) lists each individual failure as a cleanly-labelled **button** (TR 1, Generator 1-4, AC ESS, DC HOT APU, …) that arms/activates that failure via the same proven `clickElement` path the rest of the flyPad uses. The dashboard Maintenance widget also shows "No Active Failures" / the active list. The page carries the FBW caveat "Full simulation of the failures below isn't yet guaranteed." (their wording, dev build). The only rough edge is the ATA-chapter LINK labels run number+title+description together ("ATA 24Electrical Power…") — left as-is because the actionable failure BUTTONS are cleanly labelled and reworking the multi-node link text risks other flyPad pages.

**Fuel pumps + niche controls + pitch-trim correctness (post-#107 user follow-up).** (1) **Feed-tank FUEL PUMPS** — were entirely missing. The 8 cockpit pump PBs (FEED TK 1-4 MAIN + STBY) are modelled as ELECTRICAL CIRCUITS, NOT stock FUELSYSTEM pumps: state = stock `A:CIRCUIT CONNECTION ON:<id>`, set by `<id> 1 (>K:2:ELECTRICAL_BUS_TO_CIRCUIT_CONNECTION_TOGGLE)` (a TOGGLE — only fire when desired≠current). Circuit IDs from the cockpit model: FEEDTK1 MAIN=2/STBY=3, TK2=64/65, TK3=66/67, TK4=68/69. Added as Off/On combos in the Fuel panel (`_fuelPumpCircuits` map + a HandleUIVariableSet branch; the calculator-path toggle is live-verified — circuit 2 flips 0↔1). (2) **Pitch-trim correctness** — MSFSBA's "Pitch Trim" read the stock `ELEVATOR TRIM INDICATOR` (normalized −1..1), which is the WRONG representation for the A380. Fixed to read **`ELEVATOR TRIM POSITION` (radians)** and decode in `TryGetDisplayOverride` to "X.X degrees up/down" (positive = UP) — matching the A380 SD `PitchTrim.tsx` (`thsPositionRadians * RAD_TO_DEG`, `Math.sign === 1 ? 'UP' : 'DN'`). The predicted-takeoff-trim readout (`A32NX_TO_PITCH_TRIM`, ARINC429 BNR ±180 = degrees) is correct as-is. The trim WHEEL set isn't a combo (a blind pilot reads the target + actual and adjusts with the global elevator-trim keys/axis — the readouts are the accessibility win). (3) **Niche misc controls** added to the Recorder and Misc panel (settable L:vars via the catch-all): ACMS manual trigger, crew headset, service-interphone override, engine-manual-start-alternate, cabin-crew + passenger (IFE) entertainment Off, remote circuit-breaker control.

**#107 A330-Driver transcript walkthrough — accessibility gaps fixed.** Cross-referenced the full FlyByWire A380X tutorial transcript (preliminary prep → shutdown) against MSFSBA. Most procedures were already supported; the real gaps fixed: **(1) Flight-control check** — added stock surface-deflection readouts `ELEVATOR_DEFLECTION` / `AILERON_DEFLECTION` (AILERON AVERAGE DEFLECTION) / `RUDDER_DEFLECTION` + `SPOILERS_{LEFT,RIGHT}_POSITION` to the Flight Control Computers panel (live-verified the stock simvars give real degrees, e.g. elevator −20°, rudder −27.6°), so a blind pilot can sweep the stick/pedals and read each surface reach full travel (the user's explicit open question). **(2) Predicted takeoff trim** — `A32NX_TO_PITCH_TRIM` (ARINC429, the FMS-computed THS target the pilot must set before takeoff since auto-trim isn't modeled) registered + decoded in `TryGetDisplayOverride` to "X.X degrees up/down" / "Not computed". **(3) MAG/TRUE heading reference** — `A32NX_FMGC_TRUE_REF` added as a Magnetic/True combo in the Source Switching panel (live-verified settable). **(4) Brake check** — added the normal (green-system) brake pressures `A32NX_HYD_BRAKE_NORM_{LEFT,RIGHT}_PRESS` alongside the existing alternate/accumulator (the "triple indicator"; the taxi brake check wants normal ~0 while braking). RCL / TO-CONFIG-TEST buttons were already registered (ECAM control panel). **Second exhaustive transcript pass (138 items, 127 supported) — remaining gaps implemented.** Per-engine **fuel used** (`GENERAL ENG FUEL USED SINCE START:n`, kg) added to the Engines display; **rudder-trim RESET** (`A32NX_RUDDER_TRIM_RESET`) + **nosewheel-steering pedal disconnect** (`A32NX_TILLER_PEDAL_DISCONNECT`, held during the rudder flight-control check) added to the Flight Control Computers panel; **chronometer start/stop + reset** (`A32NX_CHRONO_TOGGLE`/`_RST`) added to Recorder and Misc; a new **Audio Control Panel** (pedestal) — originally the RMP-1/2 receive selectors VHF/CAB/INT/PA/NAV + volumes + transmit. **⚠️ CORRECTED 2026-06-13: only the VHF channels are real.** The FBW A380 RMP dev build models VHF + transponder ONLY (RmpPageStack routes VhfPage/SquawkPage); the HF/TEL/CAB/INT/PA/NAV receive switches, volumes and transmit selects were DEAD L:vars (the old "live-verified settable" was the write-stick trap — a write holds but drives nothing; confirmed ABSENT from the MobiFlight registered-var catalog, which lists only `A380X_RMP_{1,2}_VHF_*` + `A380X_RMP_3_PA`). The panel was PRUNED to VHF-only (VHF 1/2/3 receive + volume + transmit + screen brightness) for both seats — exposing radio controls that do nothing is worse than omitting them. NOT implemented (genuinely absent on this build): **oxygen quantity PSI** — no `A32NX_OXYGEN_*PRESSURE` L:var exists and the SD has no O2 row (the FBW dev build doesn't model crew-O2 pressure); **clock date** — `A32NX_CHRONO_DATE` reads 0 with unclear encoding (cosmetic, low value). The actual trim-*wheel set* isn't exposed (a blind pilot can't hand-set it precisely without visual feedback; the target+actual readouts are the accessibility win — read target, use trim keys/axis, read actual).

**#104 L-var catalog diff (full FBW A380 source vs MSFSBA).** Method: extracted every `A32NX_`/`A380X_` L-var token from the FBW A380 source + the cockpit model XML's actual interaction targets (`>L:` writes + `<TOGGLE_SIMVAR>`), and diffed against MSFSBA's referenced vars (`tools/_probe/fbw_lvars.txt`, `cockpit_controls.txt`, `missing_controls.txt`). The cockpit-XML interaction diff is the precise signal: **22 pilot-operable controls** existed in the cockpit but were unreferenced by MSFSBA. After triage, most were niche/maintenance/cabin (ACMS trigger, APU auto-exit test, IFE CWS/IFEC, service-interphone override, remote CB, crew headset, DLS [inop], engine-manual-start-altn) or redundant (`VENTILATION_CABFANS_TOGGLE` = the H-event for the cabin-fan PB MSFSBA already sets; `PUSH_OVHD_OXYGEN_CREW` was a false-positive — MSFSBA has it, the diff just didn't match its non-`A32NX_` prefix). The genuinely missing, valuable controls — **ADDED** (Hydraulics panel, settable via the calculator path, live-verified to actuate): the two MAIN electric hydraulic pumps **`A32NX_OVHD_HYD_EPUMPB_PB_IS_AUTO`** ("Electric Hydraulic Pump", green) + **`_EPUMPY_PB_IS_AUTO`** ("Yellow Electric Hydraulic Pump") — the cockpit's `PUSH_OVHD_HYD_ELECPUMP`/`ELECPUMPY`; and the four **engine pump DISCONNECT** PBs **`A32NX_OVHD_HYD_ENG_{1-4}AB_PUMP_DISC_PB_IS_AUTO`** ("Engine n Pumps Disconnect", `{0=Disconnected,1=Normal}`) — verified live that setting one to 0 latches `A32NX_HYD_ENG_{n}AB_PUMP_DISC`=1 (the real disconnect). Their `_HAS_FAULT` vars were already registered; only the control PBs were missing. NOTE: MSFSBA's pre-existing `EPUMPGA/GB/YA/YB_ON_PB_IS_AUTO` aux-electric-pump combos ARE real cockpit controls (8× in the XML) — kept. Readout side: the only sizeable family missing is `FQMS_*_TANK_QUANTITY` (per-tank fuel), already covered by the SD Fuel window scrape; other misses are redundant B-channel duplicates or raw input axes. The diff artefacts live in `tools/_probe/*.txt` for future re-runs.

**SURV (surveillance) controls — read + actuate via the MFD scrape.** Two pages added to `AllPages` (UIService URIs): **SURV: CONTROLS** (`surv/controls`) and **SURV: STATUS & SWITCHING** (`surv/status-switching`). CONTROLS exposes XPDR (SQWK input, AUTO/STBY, IDENT), TCAS (TA/RA / TA ONLY / STBY, ABV/BLW display range, ALT RPTG), WXR (PRED W/S, TURB, ELEVN/TILT, GAIN/MODE), and TAWS (TERR SYS, G/S MODE, FLAP MODE, GPWS) + DEFAULT SETTINGS; STATUS & SWITCHING does SYS 1/SYS 2 source switching. All controls are FBW `RadioButtonGroup` (`.mfd-radio-button` = `<label><input type=radio><span>`), inputs, and buttons — the scrape classifies them and `clickElement` actuates them via the standard path. **Live-verified the click path works:** clicking the enabled XPDR AUTO radio checked it AND cascaded to enable the TCAS sub-radios (which were `disabled` while XPDR was STBY — proper aircraft gating, not a broken click). A `disabled` radio correctly does nothing; the selected state is system-driven (a SimVar round-trip), so it updates a few frames after the click (don't expect a synchronous re-scrape to show it).

**HOLD immediate-exit / resume-hold — surfaced in the F-PLN.** On an active or decel-sequenced hold leg the MFD renders a Button into the leg's speed column (`MfdFmsFpln.renderHoldExitLine`) reading **"IMMEDIATE EXIT"** (or **"RESUME HOLD"** once exit is armed). `buildFplnLines` otherwise only emits the waypoint, so this control was invisible — it now scans each `.mfd-fms-fpln-line` for a `.mfd-button` whose normalized text is `IMMEDIATEEXIT`/`RESUMEHOLD` and emits it as its own clickable line ("Immediate exit" / "Resume hold", kind button). Enter → `onImmediateExitHold` (`fms_set_hold_immediate_exit`). Source-verified (matches `renderHoldExitLine` exactly); could NOT be live-tested because the exit line only renders on an active/sequenced leg, never on the ground (same situation as the discontinuity-delete path). Dormant no-op when no hold is active (verified the F-PLN still reads cleanly).

**Metric / imperial WEIGHT units — MSFSBA-local read-out preference, seeded from + following the aircraft (#A, redesigned).** What the FlyByWire units toggle (`CONFIG_USING_METRIC_UNIT`) actually changes, per `NXUnits.ts` (now cloned into the local fbw-aircraft sparse-checkout): **ONLY weights (kg↔lb)** and short runway/BTV/OANS distances (m↔ft) — NOT altitude (that's `A32NX_METRIC_ALT_TOGGLE`, the FCU metric-alt button, already a combo), speed, or NM route distance. So "altitude still reads 41 after toggling metric" is correct (wrong toggle for altitude). The real problem: MSFSBA reads its OWN raw kg simvars and bypasses the FMS/EFB display conversion, so the toggle had **no observable effect in any MSFSBA read-out**.
- **Source of truth = `A32NX_EFB_USING_METRIC_UNIT`** (1=kg/0=lb), the L:var the EFB `Settings/sync.ts` keeps continuously synced to `CONFIG_USING_METRIC_UNIT`. The bare `A380X_CONFIG_USING_METRIC_UNIT` / `A32NX_CONFIG_USING_METRIC_UNIT` L:vars do NOT track it (verified live). MSFSBA registers + monitors it.
- **Writing the setting:** a raw `SetStoredData('A380X_CONFIG_USING_METRIC_UNIT',…)` does NOT propagate to FBW's NXDataStore live (verified: stored=0 but the L:var + display stayed metric for 5 s+) — NXDataStore isn't reachable as a global and only its own `.set()` fires the in-process subscribers. The ONLY reliable aircraft-side write is the real EFB toggle: flyPad **Settings → Aircraft Options → "US Units"** (`setUsingMetric` → `usePersistentSetting` → `NXDataStore.set`), verified live to flip the L:var 1→0. That toggle is already accessible via the flyPad EFB (Shift+T).
- **Design:** the MCDU **Units** button (Alt+U) is therefore a **MSFSBA-local read-out preference** — `def.ToggleMetricWeight()` flips `_metricWeight` instantly (no Coherent write), and every weight read-out converts: the **gross-weight** + **total-fuel** hotkeys and the gross-weight/total-fuel **panel fields** (via `TryGetDisplayOverride`); `WeightUser(kg)` returns `(value, unit)`. The blind pilot reads MSFSBA's output, so this is what matters. `_metricWeight` (effective unit) is kept SEPARATE from `_aircraftMetric` (last L:var value) so the button and the live monitor don't fight: `ProcessSimVarUpdate` seeds both from the aircraft on first read (silent), and on a genuine AIRCRAFT change (someone flips the flyPad US Units toggle) follows it + announces "Weight units kilograms/pounds"; the button only touches `_metricWeight`.
- **General principle the user emphasised: every FBW unit/feature with an observable effect must be wired into MSFSBA's OWN read-outs — MSFSBA bypasses the cockpit displays, so display-only conversions never reach the blind pilot unless MSFSBA applies them.**

**Metric ALTITUDE — the FCU MTRS button (`A32NX_METRIC_ALT_TOGGLE`), separate from the weight toggle.** When metric-alt is ON, EVERY MSFSBA altitude read-out speaks metres (feet × 0.3048); OFF = feet. The toggle is a continuously-monitored settable combo cached into `_metricAlt` (`ProcessSimVarUpdate` returns false so the generic monitor still announces On/Off). Surfaces converted: (1) the FCU **selected-altitude** hotkey readout (`AltUser(_pAltVal)` → "FCU altitude N metres, selected/managed"); (2) the **Selected Altitude** (`FCU_ALT_VALUE`) and **Standby Altitude** (`INDICATED ALTITUDE`) panel fields via `TryGetDisplayOverride` ("N meters"); (3) the universal **current-altitude hotkeys A=MSL / Q=AGL** — gated in MainForm's `ALTITUDE_MSL`/`ALTITUDE_AGL` consumer by `currentAircraft is FlyByWireA380Definition a && a.MetricAlt` (converts feet→m and appends "meters" so the unit change is audible; the feet path stays a bare number, untouched). **Gating:** the public `MetricAlt` flag + the A380-type check mean no other aircraft and no non-metric A380 state ever hit the metric path. The standby ISIS altitude deliberately stays in feet (backup instrument).

**Fluids/quantities — verified present + accurate (units live-checked against FBW source).** HYD reservoir level GREEN/YELLOW = **gallons** (FBW's own `mod.rs` test reads `HYD_*_RESERVOIR_LEVEL` as `volume_gallon`; live ~12 gal) + LOW flag; HYD system pressure = **psi** (reads 14.7 = ambient when unpressurised on ground, i.e. real); engine oil qty ×4 (`A32NX_ENGINE_OIL_QTY:n`, fadec UNITS.Number) = **quarts** (SD `OilQuantityGauge` max = 18.3 QT, live 12–14); oil temp = celsius; total fuel + per-engine fuel-used = kg. **Oxygen pressure is NOT modelled** — `Oxygen.tsx` hardcodes crew 1829 / cabin 1854 psi (TODO in source), there is no `A32NX_OXYGEN_*` var, so it can't be read live. **Chrono elapsed IS modelled + readable (corrected — an earlier "not modelled" call was wrong).** The FBW Clock instrument writes `A32NX_CHRONO_ELAPSED_TIME` (CHR stopwatch) and `A32NX_CHRONO_ET_ELAPSED_TIME` (ET counter) in SECONDS (−1 = blank), gated on DC ESS power. The CHR is started/stopped by the **H-event** `A32NX_CHRONO_TOGGLE` and reset by `A32NX_CHRONO_RST` (NOT the K-event `A32NX.FCU_EFIS_L_CHRONO_PUSHED`, which is the ND chrono — that earlier mistest is what produced the false "not modelled"); live-verified advancing (10.8 s after toggle). The ET counter runs off the ET knob `A32NX_CHRONO_ET_SWITCH_POS` (0=Run/1=Stop/2=Reset). Both are registered and formatted in `TryGetDisplayOverride` — CHR → "M minutes S seconds", ET → "H hours M minutes", −1 → "Reset" — in the "Clock" panel.

**Metric FCU altitude INPUT.** When metric-alt is ON, `ShowFCUAltitudeDialog` treats the typed value as **metres** (range 30–14935 m), converts to the feet target the FCU actually selects (`feet = m / 0.3048`, rounded to 100 ft, `A32NX.FCU_ALT_SET`), and echoes "Altitude set to N metres, M feet". The real A380 FCU is feet internally; the MTRS window only displays the metric equivalent, so we round in feet and convert back for the read-back. Feet input is unchanged when metric is off. Heading/speed/V-S have no metric FCU mode, so only altitude input converts.

**EWD ECAM message coverage — what's already auto-announced vs what was added.** The A380X shares the A32NX's `EcamMessages` + `EclLine` rendering and even the `A32NX_EWD_*` L-var prefix (the abnormal/sensed PROCEDURES are on an in-process EventBus, no SimVar — hence the `CoherentEWDClient` DOM scrape). Already continuously auto-announced: failure **titles + action lines** (`.EclLine.AbnormalItem`, severity from Red/Amber/Cyan/White class), **memos** (left/right), **PFD memo + limitations** (string SimVars read in JS), **master warning/caution**, the full **FMA** (vertical/lateral mode + armed + autothrust via `Mon`), **AP1/2 active**, and the **SD auto-display page** (`A32NX_ECAM_SD_CURRENT_PAGE_INDEX` = the A380 equivalent of the A32NX "ECAM Warning Page" callout). **Added this pass (the genuine gap):** the bottom-of-E/WD FWS **status-area** boxes — **STS** (check STATUS page), **ADV** (advisory on SD), **FAILURE PENDING** — and the CdsDisplayUnit power-up overlays (**safety-test** / maintenance / engineering-test). `coherent-ewd-agent.js` `A.statusBoxes()` keys on the stable `.StsArea`/`.SelfTest` CSS classes (live A380X self-test text is "SAFETY TEST IN PROGRESS (MAX 30 SECONDS)"). These PERSIST, so `CoherentEWDClient` edge-detects them via `_lastStatus` (announce on appear AND on clear, seeded silently at baseline) rather than the one-shot text dedup used for failures/memos; they flow through the same `LineAnnounced` path so Ctrl+E still mutes them.

**SD pages are now DECODED into clean rows (not scraped).** The schematic SD pages scraped from `A380X_SDv2` flat-joined their X-sorted leaves and interleaved the 4 engines'/gens' values with labels ("115 V 115 APU 115 V 115") — nonsensical for a screen reader (see `Ecam screens all.txt`). Replaced with **`A380SdRows(page)`** (instance method, mirrors the A32NX `SdSystemRows`): per-page "Label: value" rows decoded from the underlying SimVars — Engine/APU/Bleed/Cond/Press/Doors/Elec AC/Elec DC/Fuel/Wheel/Hyd/F-CTL/Cruise. ARINC429 words (FQDC per-tank fuel, PRESS block-1, APU) decode via `Arinc429Word`; plain L:vars read directly; **fuel/weight rows follow the metric toggle** via `WeightUser`. `RefreshSdPageDisplayAsync(simConnect, pageIndex, ewd)` uses the decode for those pages and falls back to the scrape only for C/B / Status / Video. The ECAM-CP combo's status box auto-populates on panel show via `OnDisplayPanelShown` (no need to cycle the combo). Row vars auto-registered OnRequest in `GetVariables`.

**SD/EWD completeness + var-correctness pass (source-audited against the FBW a380x SD/EWD TSX).** Every page was cross-referenced against `fbw-a380x/.../SD/Pages/*` and the upper-EWD `EWD/*` source. **The Upper E/WD is also DECODED now** (page index 16, `ewd:true`): thrust-rating mode (`A32NX_AUTOTHRUST_THRUST_LIMIT_TYPE` → `['',CLB,MCT,FLX,TOGA,MREV]`, + FLEX temp), per-engine N1 / N1-command / EGT / N2 / N3 / FF / engine-state, then the live ECAM memo lines (from `_lastEwdCode` + `EWDMessageLookupA380`) — replacing the schematic scrape ("THR XX THR XX…"). **Wrong-var fixes that were silently reading 0/static:** PRESS outflow valves use the ARINC `..._OPEN_PERCENTAGE_B1` word (the un-suffixed name doesn't exist → 0); ELEC-DC batteries are NUMERIC-indexed `A32NX_ELEC_BAT_{1,2,3,4}_POTENTIAL/CURRENT` (3=ESS, 4=APU — the string `_BAT_ESS_/_APU_` names don't exist → 0); ELEC-DC APU bus = `A32NX_ELEC_309PP_BUS_IS_POWERED`; AC ESS bus = `A32NX_ELEC_AC_ESS_SHED_BUS_IS_POWERED` (the bare `_AC_ESS_BUS_` is AC EMER); WHEEL gear uses the L:vars `A32NX_GEAR_{CENTER,LEFT,RIGHT}_POSITION`; engine oil pressure clamps ≤0 → "not available" (genuinely not modelled on the A380 dev build). **Completeness additions:** DOORS = all 16 passenger doors via `INTERACTIVE POINT OPEN:0-15` + cargo + cockpit sliding windows; BLEED += per-engine PR/HP valve + precooler outlet temp + pack outlet temps + ram air; COND += cabin air extract + ram air; ELEC-DC += ESS/APU TRs + TR currents; ELEC-AC += STAT-INV freq, EMER-GEN load, APU-GEN-2 load, RAT; HYD += pressure-switch/reservoir-low/overheat/air-press + per-engine EDP pump PB + DISC + electric-pump active/overheat; FUEL primary source switched to `A32NX_FQMS_*_TANK_QUANTITY` (FQDC was the fallback) + per-engine/APU fuel-used + fuel-flow; F/CTL += every surface deflection (ailerons/elevators/rudders/spoilers, normalized→%) + THS pitch trim. **Failures in a status box:** the live warnings/cautions/memos ARE the Upper E/WD memo lines (decoded, clean) + the always-on auto-announce; the full INOP-SYS / STATUS / LIMITATIONS list is **EventBus-only in the FBW dev build (NOT exposed as SimVars** — the legacy `A32NX_SD_STATUS_INOP_*` L:vars are unwritten), so it surfaces only via the STATUS-page DOM scrape (the scrape fallback) when FBW renders it. Deferred (complex ARINC bit-packed discrete words, low value-per-effort): COND CPIOM cabin-fan / cargo-isolation states, BLEED pack-flow-rate gauges.

**(legacy) Reading an SD page from the ECAM-CP combo + the gap-aware scrape.** The ECAM Control Panel "System Display Page" combo (`A32NX_ECAM_SD_CURRENT_PAGE_INDEX`) drives the page via the **calculator path** (a `SimVar.SetSimVarValue` from a Coherent view does NOT switch the page — view-local/lost on disconnect; only the MobiFlight `(>L:)` write sticks); the scrape (`CoherentDisplayClient("A380X_SDv2")`, `AnnounceSdPageAsync`) remains the fallback for the non-decoded pages. `coherent-display-agent.js` now joins X-sorted leaves **gap-aware**: touching fragments (split decimals/colons like "64" "." "8") join with no space → "64.8"/"06:49:47", real values keep a space — so every display (SD/EWD/PFD/ND/ISIS) reads cleanly. Tabular pages (ENG/BLEED/HYD/COND/ELEC) come out clean; schematic pages (WHEEL/FUEL/DOOR) read flat (use the per-item SimVars for those). **To get LIVE SD data for testing**, power the aircraft up via the FBW preset: `1 (>L:A32NX_AIRCRAFT_PRESET_QUICK_MODE) 1 (>L:A32NX_AIRCRAFT_PRESET_LOAD_EXPEDITE) 4 (>L:A32NX_AIRCRAFT_PRESET_LOAD)` (1=cold&dark…4=ready-taxi engines running…5=ready-takeoff) — then the SD pages show real values. `tools/sd-page-tour.ps1` reads the current page; switch pages via the MCP/app calc write.

## VARIABLE / CONTROL TROUBLESHOOTING PLAYBOOK — UNIVERSAL (read this before saying "X doesn't work")

**This applies to EVERY aircraft in MSFSBA, not just the A380** — the FlyByWire A32NX/A380X, the Fenix A320, the PMDG 737/777, the HorizonSim 787, and any future proprietary add-on. The *mechanisms* differ per aircraft (one uses L:vars, another K-events, another a DOM bridge or a debugger socket), but the **method for finding the mechanism and proving a control works is identical**. The A380 is the worked example below because that's where we learned it the hard way; translate the specifics to whatever aircraft you're on.

**The #1 mistake this project makes repeatedly is declaring a control "broken"/"computed-output"/"reverts"/"not modelled" from a single weak test, then removing or stubbing it — and being WRONG.** It has happened on the chronometer, the Flight Director, the fuel pumps, the ECL window, the wipers, a whole batch of GPWS/recorder switches, and the MFD/KCCU interaction. Every one of those was actually fine; we just tested it wrong or assumed the hard path. The case studies at the end of this section show exactly how each false "it's broken" was overturned, so you can recognise the pattern. So:

**GOLDEN RULES**
1. **Never conclude "doesn't work" from the MCP `set_lvar` tool.** It uses a native data-def write that is UNRELIABLE for FBW L:vars and produces false reverts. ALWAYS test writes via the **calculator/MobiFlight path** — `execute_calculator_code "<val> (>L:<VAR>)"` (MCP) or `simConnect.ExecuteCalculatorCode` (app) or `SimVar.SetSimVarValue('L:VAR','number',v)` in a Coherent view.
2. **A variable can be fully working even with NO audible/visible feedback.** Many switches (GPWS modes, entertainment, NSS, service interphone) toggle and stick but the sim plays no sound and shows nothing a blind pilot notices. "I can't tell if it did anything" ≠ broken. **Confirm by READ-BACK, not by listening.** If `get_lvar` shows the new value held after ~2 s, it works — ship it.
   - **BUT: the inverse trap — a DEAD/OUTPUT-MIRROR L:var passes the read-back yet drives nothing.** Some L:vars are output mirrors the model WRITES (or legacy vars nothing reads). You write `(>L:VAR)`, it holds your value on read-back (rule above seems satisfied!), but no system reacts — because the real control is a *stock simvar* or *input event*, and your L:var is downstream scenery. **So read back the DOWNSTREAM EFFECT, not the L:var you wrote:** the stock simvar it should drive, the bus/light/valve output, the system state. If the L:var holds but the downstream value doesn't move, the L:var is dead — find the real actuator (stock event). Live-burned on this on the A380 ext-lighting (`LIGHTING_STROBE_0`, `A380X_OVHD_EXTLT_NOSE`, `A380X_OVHD_EXTLT_RWY_TURNOFF` all hold writes but the installed Asobo-template lighting ignores them — `LIGHT STROBE/TAXI` never moved; the working path was the stock `STROBES_SET`/`TOGGLE_TAXI_LIGHTS`). The prior session's "verified" nose light was this exact false positive (it read `LIGHT TAXI:2` changing — but that's the runway-turnoff index, coincidence). Conversely, a *mirror* L:var (GEN/APU-GEN `PB_IS_ON`, copied from a stock simvar each frame) makes the stickiness test LIE the other way: writing the value it already holds "sticks" trivially — to test it you must write the OPPOSITE of the current downstream simvar, or just drive the stock event and watch the mirror follow.
3. **Test EVERY state of a multi-position control, not just 0→1.** A 3-position selector (e.g. ANN LT TEST/BRT/DIM, ENGINE MODE CRANK/NORM/IGN, autobrake DISARM/BTV/LO/L2/L3/HI) must be set to each value and read back. Something can stick at 1 but revert at 2, or vice-versa.
4. **Stickiness test:** read original → write target via calculator path → **wait ~1–2 s (several frames)** → read back. Held = settable. Reverted within a frame = genuine computed output. Then RESTORE the original. (An immediate same-tick read is NOT a revert test — computed outputs revert a frame later.)
5. **The reliable existence test is the FBW SOURCE** (locally available — see the user's download path in session context, or clone it): a control var must appear in the cockpit XML/behavior templates AND have a systems-side reader — the write-stick test passes on ANY nonexistent L:var. The 2026-06 dev-source audit found six A32NX controls "verified" that way which were dead (GEN PBs, wipers, dome light, lighting presets, cargo air, ACP volumes).

**WRITE-MECHANISM DECISION TREE** (try in this order; each is live-proven on the A380):
- **Plain FBW L:var** (most controls): `<val> (>L:VAR)`. Works for switches, FD (`A32NX_FCU_EFIS_L/R_FD_ACTIVE`), ND mode/range, EFIS filters, niche toggles. This is the A380 def's catch-all in `HandleUIVariableSet` for `A32NX_`/`A380X_`/`FBW_` keys. (NOT the transponder mode — that is systems-host-managed on the stock `TRANSPONDER STATE:1` and reverts any external write; only squawk code + IDENT are settable.)
- **Stock K-event:** `SendEvent("EVENT", param)` or `<param> (>K:EVENT)`. e.g. `XPNDR_IDENT_ON`, `TOGGLE_FLIGHT_DIRECTOR` (note: the stock FD event did NOT map on this build — the L:var write did; always try both).
- **Indexed K-event:** `SendEvent("EVENT:index", val)` or multi-param `<a> <b> (>K:N:EVENT)` where N = arg count. e.g. engine anti-ice `ANTI_ICE_SET_ENGn`, ignition `TURBINE_IGNITION_SWITCH_SETn`.
- **H-event:** `(>H:EVENT)` — for things wired only to HTML events. e.g. the clock CHR: `(>H:A32NX_CHRONO_TOGGLE)` / `(>H:A32NX_CHRONO_RST)` (NOT the EFIS chrono K-event — wrong button). Verified the elapsed-time L:var then advances.
- **Electrical CIRCUIT controls** (wipers, feed-tank fuel pumps, emergency exit lights, some lights): the FBW behaviour XML drives a circuit, not a plain L:var. On/off = `<circuitId> (>K:ELECTRICAL_CIRCUIT_TOGGLE)` (state read from `A:CIRCUIT SWITCH ON:<id>`); power/speed = `<percent> <circuitId> (>K:2:ELECTRICAL_CIRCUIT_POWER_SETTING_SET)` (read `A:CIRCUIT POWER SETTING:<id>`). Fuel pumps use `<id> 1 (>K:2:ELECTRICAL_BUS_TO_CIRCUIT_CONNECTION_TOGGLE)` with `A:CIRCUIT CONNECTION ON:<id>`. **Find the circuit id in the behaviour XML** (`#CIRCUIT_ID_…#` in `model/behaviour/legacy/generated/A32NX_Interior_*.xml`), don't guess.
- **FCU values:** the A380 has NO `A32NX_FCU_AFS_DISPLAY_*` vars; use the `A32NX.FCU_*_SET` events (heading/speed/alt) and read the raw `A32NX_AUTOPILOT_*_SELECTED` SI-unit vars (convert rad→deg, m/s→kt/fpm). Signed values (V/S, FPA) must go via calculator code, not `SendEvent` (uint overflow).
- **Genuine computed outputs** (rare): a handful of overhead PBs are recomputed every frame by the FBW systems (some bus-ties). Only after the stickiness test ABOVE reverts on EVERY path do you treat it read-only — keep the read+announce, drop the set.

**WHERE TO DIG when a mechanism is unknown** (do ALL of these before giving up):
1. The live L:var catalog: `tools/_probe/fbw_lvars_clean.txt` (every L:var in the running aircraft) — grep the system name and its synonyms (e.g. wiper → also RAIN, REPELLENT).
2. The FBW **behaviour XML**: `fbw-a380x/.../model/behaviour/` — the cockpit node templates show the EXACT K/H/L mechanism and circuit ids (`awk '/Template Name="…"/,/<\/Template>/'`).
3. The **Rust systems** crate `fbw-common/src/wasm/systems/` and the **instruments** `fbw-a380x/src/systems/instruments/` (TSX) — for what publishes/consumes a var and its units (e.g. reservoir level = gallons, oil = quarts).
4. Live probe with `tools/coherent-eval.ps1 -Title A380X_SYSTEMSHOST -ExprFile <probe.js>` (reads/sets L:vars + stock simvars in-context) and the **simconnect MCP** (`get_lvar`/`get_simvar`/`execute_calculator_code`/`trigger_event`/`search_lvars`).
5. The FBW docs (docs.flybywiresim.com) for intended behaviour.

**TOOLS that exist in this repo:** `tools/coherent-eval.ps1` (Coherent eval), `tools/_probe/*.js` (probes + README), `tools/fbw_lvars_clean.txt` (catalog), the `fbw-aircraft` sparse clone at `C:/Users/franc/Documents/development/fbw-aircraft`. The simconnect MCP is the fastest write-stick tester.

**Captain/First-Officer rule:** where a control GENUINELY exists per side AND both sides work, expose BOTH as a split `… Captain` / `… First Officer` panel — never one shared control, and never invent a First-Officer var that doesn't exist. Verify each side's var is real (reads a value, not ERR) and settable before adding it. (A380 examples: EFIS, baro, FD, ND mode/range, navaids, QNH, and the RMP-1/RMP-2 audio panels.)

**GENERALISING TO OTHER AIRCRAFT.** The decision tree and "where to dig" above are A380/FBW-flavoured, but the *shape* is universal — for any aircraft, the job is (1) find the variable/event the cockpit actually uses, (2) find the write mechanism that sticks, (3) prove it by read-back. Where to look depends on the add-on's architecture:
- **FBW (A32NX/A380X):** open-source — L:var catalog, the behaviour XML, the Rust `systems` crate, the instruments TSX (everything in the `fbw-aircraft` clone). Writes via the MobiFlight calculator path or K/H events.
- **Proprietary with a SimVar/L:var surface (Fenix, PMDG):** no source — discover vars empirically. PMDG exposes a documented data struct + custom events (`send_pmdg_event`, `get_pmdg_var`); Fenix uses L:vars settable via the native data-def path (the one case where data-def IS the right write). Use the MCP `search_lvars`/`list_lvar_*`/`get_pmdg_*` to enumerate, then the stickiness test.
- **DOM/web add-ons (the A380 MFD/flyPad/ECL, any WebView/Coherent UI):** there's no SimVar — the control is in a rendered document. Read/drive it through the debugger socket (`coherent-eval.ps1`, `CoherentEWDClient`) or the WebView. Two hard-won rules: **Coherent GT (Chromium 49) allows only ONE inspector socket per page** (share the connection — that's why the ECL "showed nothing": a second socket was rejected), and a control may have **no DOM click handler** (the ECL is driven by the ECP push-button L:vars, not by clicking the lines; the MFD by the FBW `InputField` keypress path, not the KCCU cursor H-events). When a UI "can't be clicked", find what the real cockpit input actually drives underneath — don't assume the obvious element is the lever.

**CASE STUDIES — false "it's broken", and the reasoning that overturned each** (recognise these patterns):
- **Chronometer ("not modelled"):** first test pulsed the wrong control (the EFIS/ND chrono K-event) and the elapsed-time L:var didn't move → wrongly "not modelled". Reality: the clock CHR runs off the **H-event** `A32NX_CHRONO_TOGGLE` (gated on DC ESS power); fired that, the L:var advanced (10.8 s after toggle). LESSON: a var not changing means *your trigger* might be wrong, not that the var is dead — find the actual input in the source.
- **Flight Director ("writes fail, removed"):** an earlier pass wrote the engage L:var via the data-def path, saw no effect, removed the control. Reality: the **calculator-path** write to `A32NX_FCU_EFIS_L/R_FD_ACTIVE` holds (set 1 → still 1 after 2.5 s). LESSON: re-test removed controls with the calculator path before trusting an old "doesn't work" note.
- **Fuel pumps ("reverts/uncontrollable"):** the MCP `set_lvar` (data-def) appeared to revert → wrongly "computed output". Reality: feed-tank pumps are electrical **circuit connections** toggled with `(>K:2:ELECTRICAL_BUS_TO_CIRCUIT_CONNECTION_TOGGLE)`; via the calculator path they stick. LESSON: never conclude from `set_lvar`; and some "switches" are circuits, not plain L:vars.
- **Wipers ("completely inop"):** the code only set circuit *power* and never *toggled the circuit on*, so they never started. Reality (from the behaviour XML): on/off is `<id> (>K:ELECTRICAL_CIRCUIT_TOGGLE)`, speed is `<pct> <id> (>K:2:ELECTRICAL_CIRCUIT_POWER_SETTING_SET)`; both verified live. LESSON: read the cockpit node template for the EXACT sequence — a partial write looks like a dead control.
- **ECL window ("shows nothing"):** the failure monitor already held the one allowed Coherent inspector socket, so the checklist's second connection was silently rejected. Reality: share the single socket. LESSON: for Coherent UIs, suspect the one-socket-per-page limit first.
- **GPWS / recorder / NSS / entertainment ("unreliable / can't tell if it works"):** write-stick tested all of them — every one set and held after 2 s. They were never broken; the sim just plays no sound and shows nothing a blind pilot notices. LESSON: "I can't tell" is not data — read back the value.
- **MFD / KCCU interaction ("needs the cursor / can't be driven"):** assumed the MFD needed the KCCU trackball/cursor and the ECL needed DOM clicks. Reality (from the instrument source): the MFD takes text via the FBW `InputField` (focus-click + `keypress` with keyCode, Enter=13) and the ECL is driven by the ECP button L:vars — neither needs the KCCU cursor. LESSON: trace what the real hardware input writes; the visible widget is often not the thing you poke.
- **Ext lighting Strobe/Nose ("verified working" — but DEAD):** the def drove `LIGHTING_STROBE_0` and `A380X_OVHD_EXTLT_NOSE` as L:var combos; both *hold* writes, so a naive L:var read-back "passed". Reality: the installed A380X uses Asobo stock-simvar lighting templates — those L:vars are output-only/legacy and appear nowhere in the FBW source; writing 0/1/2 left `LIGHT STROBE:1`/`LIGHT TAXI:*` unchanged. The working actuators are the stock `STROBES_SET` and `TOGGLE_TAXI_LIGHTS` events (live-verified to move the simvars). The prior "verified" nose-light note read `LIGHT TAXI:2` (the runway-turnoff index, not nose) changing — a coincidence. LESSON: read back the DOWNSTREAM simvar, not the L:var you wrote; an L:var that holds but drives nothing is dead. (`A380X_OVHD_EXTLT_RWY_TURNOFF` is dead the same way — left UNexposed.)
- **GEN / APU-GEN pushbuttons ("stickiness says settable"):** `A32NX_OVHD_ELEC_ENG_GEN_n_PB_IS_ON` / `_APU_GEN_i_PB_IS_ON` are COMPUTED MIRRORS the FBW WASM copies from stock `GENERAL ENG MASTER ALTERNATOR:n` / `APU GENERATOR SWITCH:i` each frame. Writing the value they already hold "sticks" → the stickiness test falsely says settable, but a real off-command is overwritten next frame. The working control is the stock event (`TOGGLE_MASTER_ALTERNATOR` engine-index for ENG GEN; indexed `APU_GENERATOR_SWITCH_SET` for APU GEN) — verified by toggling and watching BOTH the stock simvar AND the L:var mirror follow. LESSON: when an L:var is a mirror of a stock simvar (find the `.copy(aircraft(...), aspect(L:var))` in the Rust `*_systems_wasm/src/lib.rs`), drive the stock event; keep the mirror for read/announce.
- **HYD electric-pump A/B ON/OFF ("reverts to AUTO"):** the green/yellow EMP A/B `_ON_PB_IS_AUTO` / `_OFF_PB_IS_AUTO` are toggled by the cockpit (`TOGGLE_SIMVAR`) but the FBW `A380ElectricPumpController` returns them to AUTO when the backup pump isn't needed (on the ground, EDPs pressurising). So a calc write reverts — but that is CORRECT conditional behaviour, not a dead var (the ENG-driven pumps and the two MAIN electric pumps `EPUMPB`/`EPUMPY` hold a manual command and are fully settable — the difference is the per-pump A/B controller logic). Keep them settable (probe-heat precedent); the auto-announce re-reads true state. Also: the ON button is `On/Auto` (0 = forced ON), the OFF button is `Off/Auto` — don't label the ON button OffAuto (selecting "Off" would force it ON). Each EMP genuinely has TWO physical pushbuttons, so two combos is faithful — not a unify candidate.
- **Annunciator / integral LT TEST is render-only — do NOT synthesise:** setting the ANN/INT LT knob to TEST illuminates every overhead light in the SVG but changes NO L:var (live-verified: no `_PB_HAS_FAULT`/annunciator var moves). There is nothing real to announce, so the knob just speaks its position (Test/Bright/Dim) and the real per-system fault lights announce when a genuine fault appears. LESSON: MSFSBA announces real state; if a "test"/action has no readable consequence, announce the control's own position, never a hand-written narration of what the bulbs would show.
- **Every panel control is a COMBO, not a hardware button** (screen-reader principle, user-mandated): a momentary action (TEST / ACK / RESET / chrono / rain-repellent) renders as an `Off`/`Activate` (or `Idle`/`Activate`) combo whose "Activate" option fires the pulse/H-event in `HandleUIVariableSet` (guarded on `value > 0.5`); not auto-announced (the handler speaks "<name> pressed"). The only remaining true buttons are the FCU momentary knob push/pulls (genuine knob actions with post-press value read-outs via `OnPanelButtonFired`) and value-entry fields (squawk code) — those aren't on/off switches.

**Pitch trim (`ELEVATOR_TRIM` panel display) reads `ELEVATOR TRIM POSITION` in DEGREES**, the same unit as the shared base `MON_ElevatorTrim` (Shift+T continuous trim-announce) — so no same-simvar unit mismatch. Decoded to "X.X degrees up/down" (positive = UP, matches the A380 SD PITCH TRIM block). The Shift+T trim-announce runs entirely off the base var and is unchanged on the A380 and every other aircraft (the A380 panel display is OnRequest-only and does not touch it).

**Variable provenance.** The A380X reuses the `A32NX_` prefix for almost all systems (index ranges extended: 4 engines/gens/IDGs/bleeds/FADECs, 11 fuel tanks, 16 brakes, 4 outflow valves). `A380X_` is reserved for genuinely new hardware (RMP suite, EFIS-CP/ND, fuel transfer/jettison, battery display knob, ANN/INT-LT, OIT, storm light, MFD page URIs). Source completeness from the FBW **A32NX docs** (docs.flybywiresim.com) too — MSFSBA's own A320 definition is incomplete, so don't treat it as the ceiling. Reference catalogs in `tools/`: `a380-simvars-catalog.md`, `a380-fcu-vars.md`, `a380-engine-start.md`, `a380-fault-status-vars.md`, `a380-sd-pages.md`, `fbw-a380-mfd-source-findings.md`, and the live L:var dump `_probe/fbw_lvars_clean.txt`. FCU mapping (the A380 has NO `A32NX_FCU_AFS_DISPLAY_*`/`*_LIGHT_ON` vars) is in `a380-fcu-vars.md`.

**FCU is ported from the A320** (set dialogs + paired readouts via `HandleHotkeyAction`; A380 autoflight vars). Not out of scope — it reuses the A320 `A32NX.FCU_*_SET` events with A380 value/managed/mode vars.

**A380 FCU windows (Fenix-style, input mode).** Ctrl+S/H/A/V/P/B open dedicated `Forms/FBWA380/FBWA380{Speed,Heading,Altitude,VS,Autopilot,Baro}Window` forms (shared base `FBWA380FCUWindowBase` — non-modal `ShowForm()`, focus capture/restore, Escape-to-close), replacing the old bare `ValueInputForm` dialogs (`ShowFCU*Dialog`/`ShowA380BaroSetDialog` deleted). Each form is thin UI delegating to public `FlyByWireA380Definition` methods — `SetFCU{Heading,Speed,Altitude,VS}Value`, `FireFCUButton(evt)` (Push/Pull/SPD-MACH/TRK-FPA, readback via `OnPanelButtonFired`), `RequestFCU*WithStatus` (spoken live readout on open + after each action), `RequestAutopilotStates`, `ToggleMetricAltitude`, `SetAltIncrement`, and `ApplyUIVariable` (a `HandleUIVariableSet` passthrough that looks up the `_varCache` def) — no FCU logic in the forms. The **Baro** window enters QNH ONCE and applies to both altimeters (`CAPT_QNH_SET` → `KOHLSMAN_SET` moves both); the STD/QNH toggle fires `H:A380X_EFIS_CP_BARO_PULL/PUSH_{1,2}` with state from the stock `KOHLSMAN SETTING STD:n` (the `*_EIS_BARO_IS_STD` keys remain as cache keys only — dev FBW removed those L:vars); the hPa/inHg toggle syncs both sides via `XMLVAR_Baro_Selector_HPA_{1,2}` (dev FBW honors `_1` only). The window is Fenix-style (Mode/Unit combos + value box, 2026-06). The **Autopilot** panel (Ctrl+P, previously unhandled on the A380) covers AP1/AP2, A/THR engage (`AUTO_THROTTLE_ARM`) + A/THR + AP disconnect, APPR/LOC/EXPED, with button-state labels refreshed from the cache and **FD read-only** (uncontrollable on this build). Per the screen-reader rule the windows never re-announce button presses — only value-set confirmations + readouts speak. Verify live with `tools/fcu/fcu-read.ps1` (full FCU state) / `fcu-roundtrip.ps1`; note probe-side `A32NX.FCU_*` sets are no-ops (set via the app, read back via the harness).

**FCU readouts need SI→display conversion (the A380 has NO `A32NX_FCU_AFS_DISPLAY_*` vars).** The A320 reads those pre-formatted display vars; the A380 lacks them, so MSFSBA reads the raw `A32NX_AUTOPILOT_*_SELECTED` targets, which the SimConnect data-def read returns in **SI base units**. `ProcessSimVarUpdate` converts: heading/track radians→deg (`Math.Abs(v)<=2π ? v*180/π`), FPA radians→deg (`<=0.2 ? *180/π`), V/S m/s→fpm (`*196.8503937`, round to 100), speed m/s→kt (`*1.943844`). Altitude is a SimVar read in feet already. Symptom if a conversion is missing: V/S reads "15" instead of 2000, heading "004" instead of a real bearing. FCU set/readback (`Shift+A/H/S/V`), V/S sign, and the managed-mode dot are all live-verified.

**Flight director IS controllable (corrected 2026-06) — settable per-side combos.** The earlier "uncontrollable" verdict tested the WRONG vars (`TOGGLE_FLIGHT_DIRECTOR`, `A320_Neo_FCU_FD_n_PUSH`, `A380X_EFIS_L_FD_BUTTON_IS_ON`, and the mis-named `A32NX_FCU_LEFT_EIS_FD_ACTIVE`) — all of those genuinely fail. The CORRECT vars are **`A32NX_FCU_EFIS_L_FD_ACTIVE`** / **`_R_`**, written via the calculator path: live-verified (2026-06) that `1 (>L:A32NX_FCU_EFIS_L_FD_ACTIVE)` holds (0→1, still 1 after 2 s, restored to 0). They are exposed as the "Flight Director 1/2" `OnOff` combos. The stock combined `AUTOPILOT FLIGHT DIRECTOR ACTIVE` ("FD_ACTIVE") is kept as an extra read-only status. (FD bars themselves are visual-only, but the engage toggle is real — don't rip out the combos.)

**EFIS baro is decoded for both speech AND the panel display.** `A32NX_FCU_{LEFT,RIGHT}_EIS_BARO_HPA` is an ARINC429 word (raw ~14 billion — the "altimeter 14 million" bug). The decoded value auto-announces in `ProcessSimVarUpdate` on knob turn and on STD↔QNH and hPa↔inHg unit changes, is queryable via the altimeter hotkey, AND now reads cleanly in the EFIS Captain/First Officer panels via **`TryGetDisplayOverride`** (see below) — "1013 hPa" / "29.92 inHg" / "Standard", never the raw word. Set-QNH routes through `KOHLSMAN_SET` (param = millibars×16), unit-aware. Minimums (`FM1_MINIMUM_DESCENT_ALTITUDE` / `_DECISION_HEIGHT`) likewise ARINC-decoded for both speech and the **Minimums** panel ("200 feet" / "Not set").

**EFIS baro UNIT (hPa/inHg) comes from `XMLVAR_Baro_Selector_HPA_{1,2}` (1=hPa, 0=inHg), NOT `A32NX_FCU_EFIS_*_BARO_IS_INHG`.** The IS_INHG var is stuck at 0 on the A380X (verified live via the Coherent debugger: the F/O reads `XMLVAR_Baro_Selector_HPA_2 = 0`/inHg while `A32NX_FCU_EFIS_R_BARO_IS_INHG` stays 0/hPa). The combo always wrote the XMLVAR, but the announce/display read the stuck IS_INHG — so a pilot who selected inHg kept hearing hPa. `_baroInHgL/R` is now tracked off the XMLVAR in `ProcessSimVarUpdate` (inHg when `value < 0.5`); IS_INHG is no longer registered. This feeds `BaroPhrase` and `TryGetDisplayOverride`.

**Live Coherent eval (the AI's own A380 read/write/DOM access).** The MCDU/flyPad/cockpit run in Coherent GT views exposed by the sim's remote inspector on `http://127.0.0.1:19999` (same transport `CoherentDebuggerClient` uses). You can open `ws://127.0.0.1:19999/devtools/inspector/<id>` and run `Runtime.evaluate` to scrape DOM, click elements, AND read/write ANY L:var via `SimVar.GetSimVarValue`/`SetSimVarValue` from inside a cockpit view — independent of the SimConnect MCP (which goes stale on focus loss). Resolve pages by TITLE from `/pagelist.json` (ids shift each session): flyPad EFB title-needle `- EFB`, MFD = `A380X_MFD`, ND_1 = `A380X_ND_1`, FCU = `A380X_FCU`, PFD_1 = `A380X_PFD_1`, SD = `A380X_SDv2`, EWD = `A380X_EWD`. **The convenience wrapper for all of this is `tools/coherent-eval.ps1`** (tracked in the repo — `-Title <view-needle> [-PreFile <agent.js>] -ExprFile <probe.js>|-Expr "<js>"`; its header lists every view title-needle + usage examples), and `tools/_probe/` holds a worked catalogue of probe scripts (with a `README.md`) covering every A380 feature — copy one, tweak the var/page, run it. This is how the baro-unit bug above was diagnosed, and it's the path for #43 (read verification) and #60 (write-mechanism probe). Direct `SetSimVarValue` to some XMLVARs doesn't apply same-tick — use a separate eval to read back, or the `(>L:VAR)` calculator form. The flyPad/MCDU agents expose `labelFor`/`fieldName`/`scrape`/`clickElement`/`navigateById` as methods on their `window.__MSFSBA_FLYPAD` / `window.__MSFSBA_A380` global, so an injected probe can call them to see exactly what a screen reader hears; MFD pages navigate via `navigateById(prefix,index,kccuKey)` (table = `FBWA380MCDUForm.AllPages`). **Live-verified label fixes** (found this way): flyPad value inputs read by field name (Cargo/ZFW/Passengers/Current Altitude/…) via `A.fieldName`; icon buttons via `A.tooltipSibling`; MCDU multi-span buttons space-joined via `A.spacedText` ("ACTIVATE APPR" not "ACTIVATEAPPR"); empty MFD entry fields (U+25AF boxes) read "(empty)" via `A.normEmptyBoxes`; FBW-rendered "null"/"undefined" cell text skipped; FMS-gated MFD pages (WIND/REPORT/GNSS/TIME/DATA sub-pages, disabled until a flight plan loads) return "disabled" from `navigateById`.

**`TryGetDisplayOverride(varKey, value, out text)` — panel-display decode hook.** New virtual on `IAircraftDefinition` / `BaseAircraftDefinition` (default returns false). `MainForm.UpdateDisplayText` calls it BEFORE the ValueDescriptions / numeric formatting, so an aircraft can render a decoded string for a value whose raw double isn't presentable (ARINC429 words, etc.). The A380 overrides it for the EFIS baro + minimums words. Use this for any future display field that needs unit-aware or ARINC decoding rather than re-adding raw words to a display set.

**#56 wing anti-ice + probe heat (LIVE-VERIFIED 2026-05).** Engine anti-ice uses `K:ANTI_ICE_SET_ENGn` (the L:var/XMLVAR don't drive it — verified live). WING anti-ice: the old momentary `XMLVAR_MOMENTARY_PUSH_OVHD_ANTIICE_WING_PRESSED` pulse 1→0 does NOT actuate the system (confirmed: pulsing it left `_SYSTEM_SELECTED` at 0). The combo now writes `A32NX_PNEU_WING_ANTI_ICE_SYSTEM_SELECTED` directly through the calculator path — verified 0/1 both stick; `A32NX_PNEU_WING_ANTI_ICE_SYSTEM_ON` (the valve-open output) stays the read-only "Wing Anti-Ice Flowing" status (it is gated by the on-ground inhibit, so it does not follow SELECTED on the ramp). PROBE/window heat writes `A32NX_MAN_PITOT_HEAT` (the exact var the cockpit `FBW_Airbus_Probes_Window_Heat` template toggles); it AUTO-forces ON whenever AC2 bus is powered or an engine runs, so a "set Off" reverts — that is correct A380 behaviour (probe heat is automatic), and the `Mon` auto-announce re-reads the true state. Both go through the reliable MobiFlight calculator path (the data-def `SetLVar` is unreliable for FBW L:vars).

**Disabled controls read "dimmed", and flyPad "(selected)" needs a `bg-theme-accent` sibling.** The MCDU form says `…, button, dimmed` (matching the flyPad WebView2 view and the guide), not "disabled". The flyPad agent's selected-option marker (`coherent-flypad-agent.js` `isSelectedSegment`) only fires when a SIBLING carries the unselected-segment token `bg-theme-accent` — because FBW's primary `Button` component uses the same `bg-theme-highlight` background that segmented controls use for their active option, so the bare token falsely marked every action button (Back/Apply/Reset/…) as "(selected)". (Throttle-calibration page is now FULLY relabeled + column-ordered, live-verified A320 2-axis 2026-06-05: `coherent-flypad-agent.js` `relabelThrottleCalib` + `orderThrottleCalib` qualify every duplicated/unlabeled control by axis + role — "Axis N Current Value: …", "Axis N detent low/high …" (the ProgressBar's `completedBar*Value`, tagged via `_rangeRole`), "Axis N Deadband +/-", "Axis N Set from Throttle" — and group them into Axis-1 │ detent-selector │ Axis-2 column blocks plus the TOGA/Reverser/Independent-Axes toggle bar and the Back/Reset/Load/Apply/Save bottom row. Wiring verified end-to-end: click/setValue resolve by the stamped `data-fbw-efb-idx` (`findByIdx`), and the Deadband `SimpleInput` commits via the Enter+blur dispatch in `setValue`. **Deadband is a REAL control but only a LOCAL value** — `DetentConfig.tsx` normal mode updates a local `deadZone`; the actual detent LOW/HIGH write happens on the **"Set from Throttle"** button (bounds = current `A32NX_THROTTLE_MAPPING_INPUT:n` ± deadband), then **Apply**/**Save and Apply** (`K:A32NX.THROTTLE_MAPPING_LOAD_FROM_LOCAL_VARIABLES` / `_SAVE_TO_FILE`) loads it into the throttle. So the normal-mode calibration flow is fully accessible as-is. **Known remaining gap (deferred):** the per-axis **expert-mode toggle** — the `PencilSquare` next to "Current Value" (BaseThrottleConfig.tsx, an SVG with class `text-theme-highlight` carrying ONLY `onMouseDown`) — is NOT exposed, because `classify`/`hasReactClick` only detect `onClick`. Expert mode swaps the deadband+button for direct "Configure Start"/"Configure End" number inputs (type exact bounds). To expose it: (a) classify that pencil as a button + label it ("Axis N edit detent values"), AND (b) `clickNode` must dispatch a `mousedown` (the current `click()` won't fire an onMouseDown-only handler). Normal mode works without it.)

**INIT REQUEST disabled is sim behavior, not a bug.** The MCDU INIT REQUEST (SimBrief route fetch) is dimmed until BOTH: no destination is set on the MSFS World Map (a World Map dest makes the FMS import that plan and hide INIT REQUEST) AND SimBrief/Navigraph is configured in the flyPad. The agent scrapes it correctly as "dimmed". See `docs/a380-manual.html` Part 5.

**Engine start.** ENG MASTER 1-4 = `FUELSYSTEM_VALVE_OPEN/CLOSE` (per-engine `EventParam`); engine MODE selector (MSFSBA's combo) fans `TURBINE_IGNITION_SWITCH_SET{1..4}` out to all engines via `HandleUIVariableSet` (same place the 3-speed wipers send `ELECTRICAL_CIRCUIT_POWER_SETTING_SET:141/143`).

**"Engines 3 & 4 motor but never light" — the ENGINE_COUNT=2 cockpit-knob bug + MSFSBA watchdog (2026-06, live-verified end-to-end).** Symptom: set the ENG START selector to IGN, engines 1 & 2 light, 3 & 4 motor (starter valve open, N2→~25%) but never get combustion/fuel. **Root cause (FBW source):** the `A32NX_ENGINE_MODE_SELECTOR_TEMPLATE` (`model/behaviour/legacy/Airbus.xml`) defaults `<ENGINE_COUNT>2</ENGINE_COUNT>` (A320 inheritance) and recurses `SET#ENGINE_CURRENT#` from ENGINE_COUNT down to 1 — so on installed builds where the A380 pedestal's `<ENGINE_COUNT>4</ENGINE_COUNT>` override isn't in effect, the **cockpit knob only fans ignition to engines 1+2**. Hits sighted pilots too. Diagnosed via a 5-minute live variable monitor (`tools/_probe/a380_engmon.js`, injected into `A380X_SYSTEMSHOST` via the Coherent debugger): captured `TURB ENG IGNITION SWITCH EX1:3/4` never leaving NORM(1) during a start. **The events themselves are fine** — `2 (>K:TURBINE_IGNITION_SWITCH_SET3)` / `SET4` live-lit engines 3 & 4 (combustion 1, FF 804). **THE FIX (watchdog, both files):** the def registers `ENG_MODE_SEL_POS` (= `TURB ENG IGNITION SWITCH EX1:1`, the engine-1 ignition switch the knob DOES set — NOT `XMLVAR_ENG_MODE_SEL`, which is force-driven by the physical knob and reverts external writes) as `Continuous+IsAnnounced`; `MainForm.OnSimVarUpdated` mirrors its position onto engines 3+4 via `SET3`/`SET4` on every change. So no matter how the selector moves (cockpit knob, MSFSBA combo, preset, checklist), 3+4 follow. Keys on the engine-1 var only → no feedback loop (firing SET3/SET4 changes EX1:3/4, not EX1:1). **Live-verified through the running build:** drove only `SET1`→IGN, watched EX1:3 & EX1:4 mirror to IGN with 3/4 never touched directly; drove `SET1`→NORM, 3/4 mirrored back. MSFSBA's combo (`HandleUIVariableSet` ENGINE_MODE_SELECTOR, fires SET1-4) was confirmed independently reliable — the bug only ever bites the cockpit-knob path, which the watchdog now covers.

**ARINC429 readouts.** Many SD-page quantities (FQMS per-tank fuel, FOB/GW/CG, cabin alt/VS/ΔP, APU N/EGT) are ARINC429 words — decode with `SimConnect/Arinc429Word.cs` (numeric-truncate the double to u64; low 32 bits = IEEE-754 float in engineering units; bits 32-33 = SSM, `0b11` = NormalOperation). The generic per-panel display path shows the raw double, so these are decoded for the **status-box panels** — the per-system Displays/Pedestal panels and the ECAM Control Panel's "System Display Page" combo (the dedicated `FBWA380SystemDisplayForm` window + `ShowStatusPage`/`ShowECAM` hotkeys were REMOVED — see the SUPERSEDED note below). The decode read-vars are auto-registered in the A380 def (add-if-absent loop in `GetVariables`, now in `Forms/FBWA380/EisDisplayVars.cs`).

**SUPERSEDED (2026-06) — the dedicated PFD / ND / ISIS / SD display WINDOWS in this paragraph were REMOVED on BOTH FBW jets** (commits c8db33c, 091144f, 10db641 "Remove dead … EIS / PFD display forms"; the A380 def comment near the `ReadDisplayUpperECAM` case spells it out). PFD, ND, ISIS and the System Display now read from the accessible **status-box panels** (Displays section → PFD / ND / Status; Instrument → ISIS; the SD system pages from the ECAM Control Panel's "System Display Page" combo on the Pedestal). The `ShowPFD` / `ShowNavigationDisplay` / `ShowECAM` / `ShowStatusPage` hotkeys (output Shift+P/N/U/Y) were **REMOVED app-wide** — enum entries, registrations and dispatch cases deleted (no aircraft ever handled them besides the deleted A32NX windows). `Alt+I` and the shared `ReadDisplay{PFD,ND,LowerECAM,ISIS}` actions remain but are **no-ops on the FBW jets** (still used by Fenix/PMDG). The ONE display that keeps a pop-out window is the **E/WD** (`Alt+E` → `FbwEwdWindow`, on both jets). The on-demand readout hotkeys (`ReadFlaps`/`ReadGear`/`ReadAltimeter`/`ReadGrossWeightKg`/`ReadSpeed*`/`ReadFuelQuantity`/`ReadFuelInfo`/`ReadApproachCapability`/`ReadWaypointInfo`/`ReadNDWaypoint`) and the var-name / ARINC-decode detail below remain accurate; only the *windows* are gone.

**Display read-out windows (HISTORICAL — see the SUPERSEDED note above; port of the A320 windows / Fenix-PMDG `ReadDisplay*` parity).** `FBWA380SystemDisplayForm` (SD/ECAM, ARINC429), `FBWA380NavDisplayForm` (ND — mode/range, TO waypoint via the 6-bit ident unpack, XTE/RNP/ILS), and the **shared** `Forms/A32NX/PFDForm` reused for the A380 (FMA modes, approach capability, PFD messages — all shared `A32NX_` names; PFDForm AP-status falls back to `A32NX_AUTOPILOT_n_ACTIVE` since the A380 has no FCU light vars). Wired in `HandleHotkeyAction`: `ShowPFD`/`ReadDisplayPFD`, `ShowNavigationDisplay`/`ReadDisplayND`, `ShowStatusPage`/`ShowECAM`/`ReadDisplayUpperECAM`/`ReadDisplayLowerECAM`/`ReadFuelInfo`. FMA vertical/lateral mode + approach capability also announce **live** (`Mon` vars). On-demand hotkeys ported too: `ReadFlaps`/`ReadGear`/`ReadAltimeter`/`ReadGrossWeightKg`/`ReadSpeed{VLS,F,GD,S,VS,VFE}` (full A32NX speed-tape parity; `ReadSpeedVFE`→A380 `A32NX_SPEEDS_VFEN`)/`ReadFuelQuantity`/`ReadApproachCapability`/`ReadWaypointInfo` (the last reuses the shared SimConnectManager request-370 waypoint handler). **ISIS** standby-instrument window `FBWA380ISISForm` (Alt+I / `ReadDisplayISIS`): standby attitude/heading/IAS+Mach/altitude+baro-ref/LS, read from standard air-data simvars (registered with proper units, not the generic auto-register "number") + `A32NX_ISIS_BARO_MODE` (QNH=0/STD=1, per source) / `A32NX_ISIS_LS_ACTIVE`.

**Settable temperature selectors + thrust detents.** Air-cond cockpit/cabin (18-30 C) and cargo fwd/bulk (5-25 C) temp selectors are numeric Celsius inputs (`COND_*_TEMP_SET`/`CARGO_*_TEMP_SET` keys end `_SET` → MainForm numeric box); `HandleUIVariableSet` converts °C → the FBW knob via the `_tempSelectors` table (`knob = (temp-Lo)/(Hi-Lo)*300 + Offset`). **⚠️ The CABIN knob carries a +50 Offset (cockpit/cargo = 0)** — its real range is 400-800 (NODE_ID `KNOB_OVHD_AIRCOND_FWDCABIN`), and FBW's reader/setter (`a380_systems air_conditioning/mod.rs`: reader `selected_cabin_temperature` = `knob % 400 - 50`, setter `command_cabin_selected_temperature` = `(temp-18)/0.04 + 50`) both bias it +50. Fixed 2026-06-13: without the offset the cabin landed ~2 C cold across the band (live-verified: writing 24 C → knob 200, reader `200%400-50=150` → 18+150·0.04 = 24 C exactly). The cockpit (0-300, live 75) and cargo knobs were already correct. Thrust-lever detents settable via the **Thrust Levers** pedestal panel (`THROTTLE_ALL_DETENT` + per-engine, `THROTTLEn_AXIS_SET_EX1`), and **auto-announced** on lever movement (`A32NX_AUTOTHRUST_TLA:1` monitored → `ProcessSimVarUpdate` speaks the detent reached). Manual pressurization knobs are pass-through position writes (no documented engineering-unit mapping in the dev build).

**Checklist + guides.** `Checklists/FBW_A380_Checklist.txt` (cold-and-dark→shutdown, wired in `ChecklistForm`), `docs/a380-manual.html` (the single complete screen-reader manual — cockpit/MFD/flyPad/checklists/displays/flight-planning/systems/full-flight walkthrough/hotkeys; the former `a380-mcdu-guide.md` was merged into its Parts 4–5). MCDU text entry uses the real FBW `InputField` mechanism (focus-click + `keypress` with `keyCode`, Enter=13) — NOT KCCU H-events; see `coherent-a380-agent.js`.

**Checklist hotkeys split (Shift+C vs Ctrl+Shift+C).** **Shift+C** (OUTPUT) now opens the **static text checklist** (`ChecklistForm`, which already supports `FBW_A380` → `FBW_A380_Checklist.txt`) for ALL aircraft — the A380 special-case was removed from `MainForm.ShowChecklistDialog`. The **live ECL** moved to its own key **Ctrl+Shift+C** (`HOTKEY_CHECKLIST_ECL`=9213, `MOD_CONTROL|MOD_SHIFT|0x43`, OUTPUT mode → `HotkeyAction.ShowChecklistECL` → `MainForm.ShowChecklistECLDialog`, A380-only). **ECL window UX overhaul** (`FBWA380ChecklistForm`): the checklist overlay is now **auto-shown on open** and **auto-hidden on close** (pulse `A32NX_BTN_CL`; tracked by `_weShowedOverlay`) — this is what fixed the "Checklist not reachable" error, which only ever meant the overlay was hidden (the `.EclLine` rows don't exist until C/L is toggled — verified live: after a C/L pulse the agent returns the full menu COCKPIT PREP/BEFORE START/… + abnormal procedures). The redundant Show-hide / Up / Down / Check-select **buttons were removed** (they duplicated arrows+Enter and confused the workflow); only Abnormal-procedures / Refresh / Close remain. Keys: arrows = cursor, Enter = check/select, **Backspace = Clear/back**.

**Live Electronic Checklist (ECL) — FULLY interactive accessible window (Ctrl+Shift+C on the A380).** The A380 ECL (normal checklists + active ECAM abnormal procedures) renders as `.EclLine` rows on the `A380X_EWD` Coherent view. `Forms/FBWA380/FBWA380ChecklistForm` (opened by `ShowChecklistECL` via `MainForm.ShowChecklistECLDialog`) reads every line into a navigable list that **mirrors the FWS cursor** (the `.EclLine.Selected` line), announces items as they become checked, and drives the checklist via the ECP buttons. `Resources/coherent-ecl-agent.js` (`window.__MSFSBA_ECL`) scrapes structured rows (type = headline/item/abnormal/completed; `checked`; `selected`; style = cyan-action / amber-caution / white-manual).

**CRITICAL: Coherent GT (Chromium 49) allows only ONE inspector socket per page — the ECL is read through the SHARED `CoherentEWDClient` connection, NOT its own.** The earlier claim that "the Coherent debugger allows multiple inspector connections" was **WRONG and caused the regression where the ECL window showed nothing**: opening a second WebSocket to `A380X_EWD` is rejected ("remote party closed the WebSocket connection without completing the close handshake" — verified live by holding one connection open and trying a second). Since the failure monitor (`CoherentEWDClient`) is always connected to `A380X_EWD` from A380 load, the old standalone `CoherentEclClient` could never connect → `ScrapeNowAsync` always returned empty → empty window. **Fix:** `CoherentEWDClient` now installs the ECL agent on its OWN socket alongside the E/WD agent (both are isolated-IIFE globals — verified they coexist and both scrape on one connection), exposes `EclActive` (poll-gate set by the window), `EclRowsUpdated` (pushed on change), and `ScrapeEclAsync()` (on-demand after an ECP pulse). `FBWA380ChecklistForm` takes the shared `CoherentEWDClient` (passed from `MainForm.ShowChecklistECLDialog`, which starts the monitor if needed) and never opens or disposes a connection. `CoherentEclClient.cs` was deleted; `EclRow` moved into `CoherentEWDClient.cs`. **General rule: every A380X_EWD consumer MUST funnel through the one `CoherentEWDClient` socket — never `new` a second client against the same view.**

**`EnsureConnected` must be serialized by a connect-lock (`_connectLock`, a `SemaphoreSlim(1,1)`) on `CoherentEWDClient` AND `CoherentDisplayClient`.** Both expose public on-demand scrapes (`ScrapeEclAsync`/`ScrapeDisplayAsync`; `ScrapeNowAsync`) that run on the UI thread (checklist form, RMP form's F5/debounce timer) WHILE the background `RunLoop` also calls `EnsureConnected`. Without the lock, two threads could tear down `_ws` and `ConnectAsync` concurrently, opening a SECOND inspector socket to the same Coherent page — exactly the one-socket-per-page rejection above (symptom: "display frozen / not refreshing", missed failure call-outs). The existing `_sendLock` only covers `SendAsync`, not connection setup, so it does NOT close this race — keep the separate `_connectLock` (fast-path check outside the lock, re-check inside). The public scrape methods also early-return on a `_disposed` guard so they can't re-enter connection logic on a torn-down client after an aircraft swap. The other Coherent clients (`CoherentDebuggerClient`, `CoherentNDClient`, `CoherentEFBClient`) call `EnsureConnected` only from their single `RunLoop`, so they don't need it (add one if you ever expose a public on-demand scrape on them). Relatedly, every form that marshals a background bridge-push to the UI thread (`FbwEfbForm`, `FBWA380MCDUForm`) does so via a `SafeBeginInvoke` helper that wraps `BeginInvoke` in `try/catch (InvalidOperationException)` — the `IsHandleCreated` check alone races a concurrent handle-destroy (aircraft swap / window close), and the throw would otherwise be unobserved on the pool thread. (`ObjectDisposedException` derives from `InvalidOperationException`, so one catch covers both.)

**Every Coherent client's `EnsureConnected` must (a) re-install the agent on a still-open socket instead of reconnecting, and (b) Abort+Dispose any existing socket BEFORE `ConnectAsync`.** A 5-s eval timeout clears `_agentInstalled` while the socket stays open; without (a)+(b) the next cycle opened a SECOND inspector socket to the same page — Coherent accepts then closes the handshake, `_ws` is replaced, and the healthy old socket is orphaned with no way to release the page for the rest of the process (the EWD failure monitor was the worst casualty). All five clients now carry the pattern (ported from `CoherentDisplayClient`); keep it when adding a sixth. The EWD's ECL/display sub-agents additionally self-heal by re-installing inside `ScrapeEclAsync`/`ScrapeDisplayAsync`, and the SD Upper-E/WD fallback must NEVER construct a second `CoherentDisplayClient("A380X_EWD")` while `EwdMonitor` exists.

**Interaction — the ECP buttons FULLY drive the ECL (verified live end-to-end; NOT cursor-limited).** The `.EclLine` rows have no DOM click handlers (pointer-events-free SVG over `ewd-main`), so interaction goes through the real ECP push-button L-vars, which `FwsCore.ts` buffers each cycle into pulse nodes and `FwsNormalChecklists.ts` acts on: `A32NX_BTN_CL`→show/hide; `A32NX_BTN_UP`/`_DOWN`→`moveUp`/`moveDown` (cursor in the menu AND inside a checklist); `A32NX_BTN_CHECK_LH`/`_RH`→ on the menu (`checklistId===0`) `navigateToChecklist(keys[selectedLine])` **opens** the selected checklist, inside a checklist `checkSelected()` **ticks** the selected manual item and auto-advances; `A32NX_BTN_CLR`→`navigateToParent`; `A32NX_BTN_ABNPROC`→abnormal list. **Precondition (FwsNormalChecklists ~L451):** `if (!checklistShown) return;` — Up/Down/Check do nothing until `C/L` shows the checklist (this is why an earlier test "didn't move the menu"; the earlier "needs the KCCU cursor / FBW #9348" conclusion was WRONG). The form pulses these via the MobiFlight calculator path (`1 (>L:…)`/`0 (>L:…)`); its list-box Up/Down arrows drive `BTN_UP`/`_DOWN` and Enter drives `BTN_CHECK_LH`, so the reader's selection always mirrors the cockpit cursor. Sensed items tick themselves; manual items tick on Check. Verified live: C/L showed the menu (BEFORE START selected) → DOWN→AFTER START → CHECK opened it (cursor on ANTI ICE) → CHECK ticked ANTI ICE and advanced to PITCH TRIM → navigated to RESET + CHECK reset it. The KCCU keys are H-events `H:A32NX_KCCU_L_<KEY>` (ESC/DIR/ENT/UP/DOWN/…) consumed by the MFD, not needed for the ECL. The A380 ECL does its own sensing (`skipCompletedSensed`), so sensed items tick themselves.

**Two SEPARATE checklist systems — don't confuse them.** (1) The **E/WD ECL** above is the real aircraft checklist (FWS-driven) — this is what MSFSBA's Checklist hotkey opens and what matters for flying. (2) The **flyPad EFB Checklists page** (`/checklists` tab) is a *separate, tablet-only tracker*: the A380 DOES mount the shared `fbw-common` Checklists page (verified — earlier "A380 has no EFB checklist page" was wrong; only the *Pages* subdir is A380-specific, the page itself is shared via `EfbWrapper`/`ToolBar`), but ticking a flyPad item writes **only EFB-local Redux state** (`trackingChecklists`), never an aircraft L-var/SimVar — it does NOT drive the E/WD ECL. The persistent setting `EFB_AUTOFILL_CHECKLISTS` (real stored key **`A380X_EFB_AUTOFILL_CHECKLISTS`**; prefix = uppercased `AIRCRAFT_PROJECT_PREFIX`=`A380X`, confirmed live via `A380X_CONFIG_USING_METRIC_UNIT`) flips the flyPad page from manual ticking to read-only auto-sensing: every 1 s the EFB evaluates each item's `condition` (SimVar/L-var compares from `config/a380x/a380-842/checklists.json5`) and auto-marks matches. Set it through the EFB store: in the `- EFB` Coherent view, `SetStoredData('A380X_EFB_AUTOFILL_CHECKLISTS','1')` (persists; same store the Realism settings toggle writes). It only affects the tablet, not the aircraft.

**STATUS / INOP SYS / LIMITATIONS (#2) — REACHABILITY SOLVED via the systems-host FwsCore; data still FBW-WIP.** The earlier "EventBus-only, unreachable" conclusion was wrong. Each FBW instrument is a custom element whose JS instance/objects are reachable from the debugger: `document.querySelector('a380x-mfd').fsInstrument` exposes `bus` + `fmcService` (full flight plan via `fmcService.master.flightPlanInterface.active.allLegs`), and **`document.querySelector('systems-host').fwsCore`** (on the `A380X_SYSTEMSHOST` view) exposes the FWS directly: live Subjects `inopSysAllPhasesKeys` / `inopSysApprLdgKeys` / `inopSysRedundLossKeys`, `limitationsAllPhasesKeys` / `limitationsApprLdgKeys`, `ecamStatusNormal`, `presentedAbnormalProceduresList` / `activeAbnormalNonSensedKeys`, and `pfdMemoLines` / `pfdLimitationsLines` (each `.get()` / `.value`). So the channel is OPEN — a future systems-host agent can read these and map the keys to text (EcamInopSys/EcamLimitations dicts) and announce them. BUT the dev build still doesn't POPULATE inop/limitations even on failures (verified: PRIM 1 failure left `inopSysAllPhasesKeys.get()` `[]`, `ecamStatusNormal` true) — that computation is WIP on FBW's side, out of our control. So integrate the reader when FBW ships the data; today it would surface empty (the abnormal *procedures* already come through the ECL, and per-failure "FUNCTIONS NOT AVAIL" through the failure-procedure scrape). **General lesson: the per-instrument `fsInstrument`/element objects (bus, fmcService, fwsCore) are the master key to anything previously deemed "not exposed".**

(Original note kept for context:) The PFD/E/WD LIMITATIONS come through the `A32NX_PFD_LIMITATIONS_LINE_1..8` string SimVars already read by the E/WD monitor (see PFD memo+limitations above); the E/WD also renders a `.LimitationsContainer`. The INOP-SYS list is EventBus-only (no SimVar). Live-tested with cabin-fan AND PRIM 1 failures: the FBW A380 dev build does NOT yet populate limitation text, PFD-limitation strings, or any INOP/STATUS DOM area (the limitations/abnormal-status system is WIP — many procedures show "(WIP)"). So #2's data channel is in place and will surface automatically once FBW computes it; there is nothing more to scrape today (the per-failure "FUNCTIONS NOT AVAIL" is already captured by the failure-procedure scrape).

**flyPad Dashboard ("Your Flight") — column-aware reading order.** The EFB Dashboard is a two-column flex layout (`fbw-common Dashboard.tsx`: one `flex w-full` row of two `w-1/2` columns): LEFT = `FlightWidget` ("Your Flight"), RIGHT = `RemindersWidget` ("Important Information": Weather / Pinned Charts / Maintenance / Checklists, order from persistent `REMINDER_WIDGET_ORDERED_KEYS`). The generic row-by-row, left-to-right enumerate in `coherent-flypad-agent.js` interleaved the two columns into a jumble. Fix: `enumerate()` detects the dashboard via `A.isDashboard(root)` (an `<h1>` containing "Your Flight") and, for that page only, sorts by **column first** (`_col` = left/right of `rootRect.width*0.48`, nav-rail still last) then row then left — so it reads the whole left widget, then the whole right widget. Other pages keep the row-wise order (so a Settings name+toggle stay paired). Widget/section titles are already captured as `h1.font-bold` / `h2.font-medium` headings, so each block reads under its own title.

**flyPad SETTINGS — dedicated builder `A.buildSettingsLines` (2026-06, A380 + A320, shared).** The `/settings/<category>` detail pages flowed through the generic pass and read cluttered (loose option buttons, inputs that borrowed a neighbour's label, the current value folded into the label, the Audio rc-slider internals as phantom "slider" lines, the page label doubled, and every index category falsely "(selected)"). `buildSettingsLines` (invoked in `enumerate`'s builder chain after `buildChartLines`) OWNS the settings rows wrapper (`A.settingsContentRoot` = the `div.divide-y-2` right of the category column; bails on the throttle Calibrate page via its "Axis N for Throttle" h1) and re-emits one clean line per control. Row discovery: `A.settingUnits` scans every `flex-row` whose FIRST child is a plain text label (`hasClassToken`, not substring) and whose SECOND child is the control cell — this handles the `div.py-4` wrappers AND the **compound** py-4 (two settings in one wrapper, e.g. A380 "Auto Cabin Lighting" toggle + "Cabin Lighting Brightness" slider). Per unit: SelectGroup (`A.selectGroupOptions` = the `span.cursor-pointer` option leaves; selected via the existing `isSelectedSegment`) → name line + tight option buttons; Toggle (`A.toggleNode` reuses `classify(el)==="toggle"`) → checkbox; SimpleInput / rc-slider+input (Audio) → one labeled `A.emitSettingInput`; action/sub-page link → "<row name>: <verb>". **OWNERSHIP GATE (graceful degrade — the A320 safety net):** `buildSettingsLines` checks `A.settingUnitHasControl` across the units and returns `null` (does NOT own, defers to the generic pass) when the region has no recognizable control — so an info page (About) keeps its values AND a layout the builder doesn't recognize (e.g. an A320 variant) degrades to the readable generic output instead of an owned-but-blank page. Global helper fixes: `pageLabel` returns `head` alone when it already starts with "Settings - " (de-double); the `(selected)` suffix in `enumerate` is gated `!/^\/settings\//.test(hrefAttr)` (the index category cards all carry the `bg-theme-accent` BASE token, so `isActiveTab` over-reported all 8). Regression harness: `tools/flypad-settings-test/` (jsdom, live-baked `data-rect`/`data-vis` fixtures; `node --test`). **Verified live on BOTH the A380 and the A32NX** (2026-06-06: full Settings tour + doors open/closed/in-transit with precise names + the door-fiber enum inventory). A320 regression coverage is locked in (`a320.test.js` + the `a320-*` fixtures; `node --test` = 39/39). Only a human NVDA pass remains.
