**flyPad DOORS read open/closed, with precise names + grouping in flight (2026-06, A380 + A320).** Ground-service DOOR tiles now read **open / closed / in transit** (user request) instead of the generic "(active)" / silence. `A.doorOpenState(n)` climbs to the cursor-pointer tile WRAPPER and maps its `serviceState` colour: green=open, amber=in transit, none=closed (source-confirmed: `A380Services.tsx`/`A320Services.tsx` set `ServiceButtonState.ACTIVE` = `bg-green-700` exactly when `INTERACTIVE POINT OPEN === 1`). The door block in `enumerate` applies this to door tiles whether they're an operable **button** (on the ground) OR a disabled **heading** (in flight — FBW sets `opacity-20 pointer-events-none` and drops the DOM onClick, so only the inner `<h_>` classifies). **Precise name while disabled = fiber-aware `doorIdentity`:** when the DOM/`__reactProps` onClick is gone, FBW still PASSES the onClick closure (carrying the const-enum `/* Main1Left */` comment) as a React prop, so it survives in the **fiber** — `doorIdentity` now walks `__reactFiber$….memoizedProps.onClick` up the return chain (~1 hop, only this door's handler is in its own ancestry) and parses the enum → the precise `DOOR_NAMES` label (A380 "Main Door 1 Left"…; A320 "Forward Left Door"…), in flight too. The left/right COLUMN fallback stays button-only (don't invent a side for a disabled heading). `orderGroundServices`' door-grouping band (150) now includes `kind==="heading"` doors so they group together in flight, not scattered among the trucks. **The fiber naming is live-only (jsdom has no React fibers) — `tools/flypad-settings-test/doors.test.js` covers `doorOpenState` + grouping + the active/called scoping, but the precise-name path is verified in the sim.** Probe: `tools/_probe/_door_fiber.js`.

**A380 MFD company-route (SimBrief) insertion — verified live.** After requesting on the FMS INIT page, the scratchpad shows "COMPANY F-PLN RECEIVED WAITING FOR INSERTION" and the top-right button reads **"RECEIVED CPNY F-PLN"**. Clicking it opens a dropdown with **`INSERT*`** (and `CLEAR*`); `INSERT*` calls `fmc.insertCpnyFpln(Active)` → copies the Uplink plan straight into the Active plan (no TMPY for the uplink itself). FLT NBR / FROM / TO / ALTN come pre-filled from SimBrief and stay editable afterwards (no TMPY, Preflight). Runway+SID selection IS a TMPY (DEPARTURE→RWY→SID→`INSERT TMPY *`). MSFSBA drives all of this through the existing `__MSFSBA_A380.clickElement(idx)` path — the elements (button, then the `INSERT*` menu item) appear in the normal scrape. Verified live: requested → RECEIVED CPNY F-PLN → INSERT* (VCBI→OMDB, ALTN OMAA, FLT NBR UAE111, CRZ FL380, CI60) → DEPARTURE → RWY 22 → SID BASU1D → INSERT TMPY.

**MCDU readout polish.** Empty *editable* MFD fields now read **"blank"** (not "(empty)") — `coherent-a380-agent.js` `normEmptyBoxes`/`elementLabel`/`lineText` emit `blank`; disabled fields still show their native dashes (`----`). The leading element-index number (`"11: …"`) was dropped from `FBWA380MCDUForm.RefreshDisplay` — it was an internal click handle (`el.Index`, still used to click), not a user input, and the trailing role word ("…, button" / "…, edit") already marks actionable lines.

**MFD grid pages — row merge + dedicated F-PLN builder.** Grid pages render each cell as a separate absolutely-positioned text node, so `enumerateLines` was emitting one cell per line (token-salad). General fix: after the row-sort, the agent MERGES consecutive same-row STATIC-TEXT cells (same `top` bucket) into one line joined with **", "** (comma → screen-reader pause). Interactive controls (`idx>0`) always keep their own line. Leg distances get **"NM"** appended (DIST-column class `mfd-fms-fpln-leg-upper-row` + pure-integer pattern; track has `°`, FPA has a sign, so neither matches). This serves PERF / FUEL&LOAD.

**The F-PLN has its OWN per-waypoint builder** (`A.buildFplnLines`), because the row merge still scattered it (waypoint cells and leg cells sit at different y within one `.mfd-fms-fpln-line`). Each `.mfd-fms-fpln-line` container groups a waypoint with its INBOUND leg + constraints; the builder folds it into **one clean line**: `IDENT, via AIRWAY, N NM, track T°, <constraint>, ETA hh:mm` — dropping empty/dash predictions, stripping the `@` overfly marker, deduping the repeated procedure name (via X once until it changes), and decoding constraints (`+N`→"at or above N feet", `-N`→"at or below N feet"). `enumerateLines` calls it when `.mfd-fms-fpln-line` exists and then skips the whole plan grid in the generic pass via `A.insideFpln` (any ancestor class containing `mfd-fms-fpln`); the header row is dropped (each line is self-describing). Builder items carry `fpln:true` so the merge never touches them. Verified live: the VCBI→OMDB plan reads "DER22, via BASU1D, 2 NM, track 217°" / "BI613, 5 NM, track 294°, at or below 5000 feet" / "TVM, via P570, 80 NM, track 294°". The F-PLN shows a WINDOW of ~12 waypoints with DEST pinned at the bottom — page down (Ctrl+Down) to walk the rest of the route (documented in docs/a380-manual.html Part 4).

**F-PLN EFOB / T.WIND view (the column-header toggle).** The F-PLN page's two right-hand columns toggle between SPD / ALT and **EFOB / T.WIND** via the header button (`MfdFmsFpln` `efobOrSpeed`/`windOrAlt`; button text "EFOB…T.WIND" when active). `buildFplnLines` detects the mode from `.mfd-fms-fpln-button-speed-alt` (text contains "EFOB") and parses those columns accordingly: in EFOB mode it reads **EFOB** (the speed cell, tonnes "NN.N" → `EFOB 36.5`) and the **wind** (the altitude cell: direction `ddd°`/`TAIL`/`HEAD` + `/` + magnitude knots → `wind TAIL/7`). Before this, SPD/ALT parsing ran unconditionally, so EFOB was dropped (decimal failed the speed regex) and the wind magnitude was mis-emitted as a "speed". **Wind direction & magnitude each render as a ditto-mark (`"`) when unchanged from the line above** (`formatWind`); the builder carries `prevWindDir`/`prevWindMag` forward to resolve them (a line-by-line reader can't glance up), and strips the FBW zero-padding (`007`→`7`). The altitude constraint-marker block is skipped in EFOB mode. SPD/ALT mode is byte-for-byte unchanged. Live-verified on the OMDB approach window (every leg reads ETA + EFOB + wind). A headwind shows the literal word `HEAD` (tailwind `TAIL`), not a glyph — `formatWindPredictionDirection` returns `prediction > 0 ? 'TAIL' : 'HEAD'` for an along-track component, else the true-degrees heading.

**F-PLN waypoint lines are CLICKABLE → lateral-revision menu (incl. clearing a discontinuity).** Clicking a `.mfd-fms-fpln-line-ident` via plain DOM `.click()` opens the real MFD **revisions menu** (`.mfd-context-menu` of `.mfd-context-menu-element` items: FROM P.POS DIR TO, INSERT NEXT WPT, DELETE \*, DEPARTURE, ARRIVAL, OFFSET, HOLD, AIRWAYS, OVERFLY \*) — no KCCU cursor needed (verified live via `__MSFSBA_A380.clickElement(idx)`). The menu items were already captured as kind `menu`→role "option", so the only gap was the lines themselves. `A.buildFplnLines` now (a) stamps each waypoint's ident cell with the `data-fbwa380-mcdu-idx` and emits it as kind **`fplnwpt`** (role word "waypoint", form `RoleWord`), so Enter on a waypoint opens its revision menu (then `ScheduleRefresh` shows the options); and (b) handles **special lines** (`.mfd-fms-fpln-line-special`, source `renderSpecialLine`: a delimiter band `- - - DISCONTINUITY - - -` with NO ident child). Those were previously DROPPED by `if(!ident) continue` — so a **discontinuity was invisible** to the reader. Now the label is surfaced; a `DISCONTINUITY` line is stamped on the line div itself (which carries the same `onIdentClicked` handler) and emitted as kind **`fplndisc`** (role "button"), so Enter→menu→**DELETE \*** clears it (calls `flightPlanInterface.deleteElementAt(legIndex,false,…)`). Other markers (END OF F-PLN…) stay plain text (their click opens nothing). `buildFplnLines` now threads/returns the `idx` counter; the merge step already skips `fpln:true` items so clickable lines keep their own row. This is the non-redundant path: a flight-plan **edit** (clear disco, DIR TO, HOLD, insert/delete) is impossible via SimVars and had no prior MSFSBA route. Source: `fbw-a380x/.../F-PLN/MfdFmsFpln.tsx` + `FplnRevisionsMenu.tsx`. (No live disco existed in the test plan to click — waypoint path verified end-to-end live; disco path is the identical handler, source-verified.)

**Combo boxes announce expanded / collapsed.** MFD dropdowns (RWY/APPR/STAR, source selectors, etc.) now read their open state, e.g. "RWY: 30R, combo box, collapsed" → Enter → "…, combo box, expanded" (and the option list folds in as `option` lines). Detection (verified live): the FBW DropdownMenu button gains an **`opened`** class and its sibling `.mfd-dropdown-menu` flips to **`display:block`** when open (`MsfsAvionicsCommon/UiWidgets/DropdownMenu.tsx`). `coherent-a380-agent.js` `A.comboExpanded(n)` walks ≤6 ancestors for an `opened` class or a `.mfd-dropdown-container`'s menu `display`, returns true/false; `enumerateLines` sets `expanded` (true/false for combos — kind `dropdown` or isChoice input — else null). Wire-through: `ScrapeElement.expanded` (`bool?`) → `CoherentDebuggerClient` emits `items.N.expandstate` = "expanded"/"collapsed"/"" (and folds it into the change-hash so a toggle re-renders) → `FBWA380MCDUForm.McduElement.ExpandState`, appended after the role word in `RefreshDisplay`. Non-combo controls send "" (no state). Verified live on ARRIVAL: 5 dropdowns report `false` collapsed, the expanded APPR reports `true`.

**Open menu/combo options are placed directly UNDER the control that opened them.** A popped-up combo/context menu overlays other content, so the geometric sort scatters its options between unrelated lines. `enumerateLines` tags each option with `menuGroup` (container index into `menuConts`) + `menuOrder` (DOM order), then a final regroup pulls each menu's options into one contiguous block (menu order) and inserts it **immediately after its opener** (NOT at the top — the user asked for "right under the combo"). Opener resolution (`triggerIdxFor`): a **combo box** → the stamped control in the same `.mfd-dropdown-container` as the open `.mfd-dropdown-menu` (skip the option elements via `ancestorWithClass(...,'mfd-dropdown-menu')`); a **F-PLN waypoint/discontinuity revision** (`.mfd-context-menu`) → the F-PLN line whose ident the FWS marked **`.selected`** (`MfdFmsFpln` `selectedForRevision.sub` adds class `selected` to the `identRef`); fallback `.mfd-button.opened`. A group whose opener can't be found falls back to the top. Verified live: expanding "F-PLN INFO" lists ALTERNATE/CLOSEST AIRPORTS/FIX INFO/… right under it; opening DER22's revision lists DIR TO/INSERT/DELETE*/HOLD/… right under DER22, then the route continues.

**Combo boxes announce their SELECTED value.** A DropdownMenu combo carries its value in `.mfd-dropdown-inner` (already read). Button-style dropdowns (ARRIVAL/DEPARTURE RWY/APPR/STAR/TRANS) have NO inner value — the field name is the button text and the selection sits in a summary grid directly beneath the matching header. `A.comboSelectedValue(label, node)` finds the header text cell equal to the button label, then reads the value cell immediately below it (≤45px, x-overlapping); dashes → "" (unset). `A.lineText` folds it in so the combo reads "RWY, 30R" not bare "RWY" (verified live: RWY→"30R", APPR/VIA/STAR/TRANS→unset). Combined with the expand-state this reads e.g. "RWY, 30R, combo box, collapsed".

**MFD pages tidy-up sweep (2026-06-04) — generic scrape cleanups in `coherent-a380-agent.js`, all jsdom-tested (`tools/perf-builder-test`, 12 tests; fixtures captured live) + live-verified; selectability invariant preserved (every input/combo/radio/subtab/button/surv keeps its stamped idx).** The sweep cleaned every accessible MFD page + F-PLN sub-page + per-page sub-tab. Builders (run in `enumerateLines` after `buildFplnLines`/`buildPerfLines`):
- **`buildLabeledFields`** (all pages) — one clean `LABEL: value unit` per `.mfd-label-value-container` with an INNER `.mfd-label` (GW/CG/FOB, EPU, GPIRS POSITION, …); owns the container so the static pass skips it.
- **Label-aware Y-merge composer** — sibling label/value/unit data rows compose as `T.TRK: 134.4 °T, T.HDG: 134.4 °T` (a real label = `.mfd-label` with letters, non-unit, starts a `, ` group + binds its first value with `: `; a bare unit attaches with a space; a leading `FL` binds its level → `FROM CRZ: FL 390`). The "real label" guard stops a number/time cell that carries `.mfd-label` (FUEL&LOAD DEST/ALTN prediction grid) from spuriously binding.
- **`buildSurvControls`** (gated `isSurvPage`) — prefixes each SURV CONTROLS radio/SurvButton with its nearest column header above (x-overlap): `XPDR: AUTO`, `TCAS: TA/RA`, `WXR: AUTO`, `TERR SYS: OFF: ON`, `ELEVN/TILT: AUTO`; matched headers owned (not double-read). TCAS ABV/BLW/NORM range column has no DOM header → bare.
- **`.mfd-surv-status-item` never row-merges** (`isStatusItem` flag) — STATUS & SWITCHING status cells each read on their own line; no false `TAWS: TERR SYS OFF` heading-bind.
- **Orphaned trailing-unit re-attach** — a static line that is JUST a unit (`°`/`KT`/…) folds onto the value line above when that ends in a number/%, fixing the Y-bucket rounding split (NAVAIDS SELECTED `SLOPE: -3.0` + stray `°` → `SLOPE: -3.0 °`).
- **D-ATIS** function selector (`.mfd-button` in `.mfd-dropdown-container`, no `.mfd-dropdown-inner`) reads `UPDATE OR PRINT` via `spacedText`; `comboSelectedValue` now skips `.mfd-atccom-datis-block-msgarea` + any text > 40 chars so it can't absorb the ATIS report. ATIS reads once as its own line.
- **F-PLN**: dropped the stray `at * feet` (constraint cell can hold a bare `*` managed-marker — require a digit); **STEP ALTs** subtab relabels the two anonymous fields to `Step waypoint` / `Step altitude`.
- Sub-pages swept (read fine, no change): LAT REV menu, DEPARTURE (`RWY, 24L`/`SID, OSHNN1`/`TRANS, BEALE` via comboSelectedValue), ARRIVAL, HOLD, AIRWAYS, CONSTRAINTS(VERT REV/ALT), VERT REV/SPD, DATA→FMS P/N, NAVAIDS→SELECTED FOR FMS NAV, DATA/AIRPORT→PILOT STORED RWYs. NOTE: HOLD/AIRWAYS/DEPARTURE-ARRIVAL-selection/SPD create a TMPY on interaction — erase after (ERASE TMPY on F-PLN). Recon + per-page status: `tools/_probe/captures/mfd_pages_recon.md`.

**`FBWA380MCDUForm` window UX (Shift+M).** Page buttons reorganised: row 1 (FMS) INIT/F-PLN/PERF/**FUEL&LOAD (Alt+L)**/RAD NAV/SEC FPL/DIR; row 2 ATC COM/**SURV (Alt+V)**/CLR/Refresh/Units. The **UP/DOWN page-step buttons were removed** (their job is Ctrl+Up/Down + PageUp/PageDown — kept); FUEL&LOAD + SURV are additive (fill the freed slots), ATC COM KEPT (only quick path to D-ATIS + the CPDLC MSG RECORD read). **Units mnemonic moved Alt+U → Alt+N** (Alt+U clashed with the old UP button — a shared mnemonic only cycles focus). The **"go to MFD page" combo is debounced (350 ms)** — a closed DropDownList fires `SelectedIndexChanged` per arrow, so without it arrowing F-PLN→INIT loaded+announced every page between; now it navigates once when the selection settles (`PageNavTick`), making the combo a clean fast-path to all 30 pages. **CLR (`PerformClear`, on Alt+C AND Backspace) now also dismisses a displayed footer info/error MESSAGE** — matching real Airbus CLR (clears the scratchpad message before acting on a field): staging scratchpad text → else a footer message shown (`_previousScratchpad` non-empty + a `CLEAR INFO` element on the page, `FindClearInfoIndex`) → click CLEAR INFO ("Info cleared") → else selected field → else KCCU backspace. `CLEAR INFO` (the MFD's footer-message button) is DISTINCT from clearing a field — that's why it needed wiring.

**Silent on first aircraft detect.** Aircraft-specific `ProcessSimVarUpdate` branches announce directly (bypassing the `simVarMonitor` 5s grace), so the A380 altimeter setting spoke on first detect (its `_lastBaroL`/`_baroStdL` caches start at sentinels, so the first real sample read as a change). Fix is global + minimal: `ScreenReaderAnnouncer.Suppressed` drops the AUTOMATIC paths (`Announce`/`AnnounceQueued`/`AnnounceWithQueue`) but NOT `AnnounceImmediate` (user hotkeys still talk); `MainForm` sets it true on connect and false when the existing 5-second grace timer fires (`MainForm.cs:457-467`). The per-var caches still update under suppression (branches run, just don't speak), so the FIRST post-grace change announces correctly. Consistent with the existing `_tlaBaselineDone` thrust-lever suppression and the `simVarMonitor`/ECAM grace.

**D / Shift+D distance hotkeys (FMS progress).** PMDG-style: **D** = distance to destination, **Shift+D** = distance to Top of Descent. The A380 has no PMDG SDK struct and no stock SimVar for these, so they come from the MFD's FMS guidance controller via the Coherent debugger. `coherent-a380-agent.js` `A.flightInfo()` returns `{distToDest, distToTD, distToTC, timeToTD, timeToTC}` (JSON): `distToDest` = `guidanceController.alongTrackDistancesToDestination.get(0)` (active plan, works on the ground — verified 1810 NM VCBI→OMDB); `distToTD/TC` derived from `currentPseudoWaypoints` (ident `(T/D)`/`(DECEL)`/`(T/C)`, `distanceFromStart`) via `toGo = distToDest - (totalPlanDist - pwp.distanceFromStart)`, where `totalPlanDist` = last leg `calculated.cumulativeDistance` — these are null until airborne (FMS computes the descent in flight). Wiring: the keys are already globally bound (`HotkeyManager` D=0x44 / Shift+D → `ReadDistanceToDest`/`ReadDistanceToTOD`, the same actions the 787 uses) → `FlyByWireA380Definition.HandleHotkeyAction` casts `parentForm` to `MainForm` and calls `MainForm.AnnounceA380FlightInfo(tod)` → async `CoherentDebuggerClient.EvalForResultAsync("__MSFSBA_A380.flightInfo()")` → parse + `AnnounceImmediate`. **Shift+D also announces the TIME to top of descent** — `flightInfo()` adds `timeToTD`/`timeToTC` from the matched pseudo-waypoint's `flightPlanInfo.secondsFromPresent` (the FMS's OWN time-to-go, which accounts for the descent/decel/wind profile — more accurate than distance/ground-speed; null until the FMS computes the descent), and `MainForm.FormatEtaSeconds` formats it as `": HH:MM:SS"` to match the PMDG TOD readout EXACTLY (mirrors `PMDG737Definition.FormatEtaFromDistance`), e.g. **"145 miles to top of descent: 00:16:58"** — live-verified in flight. Destination ETA/EFOB still not included. **The A32NX has the SAME D/Shift+D readout** (added later; identical wording/format). It reads its OWN FMS guidance controller — `document.querySelector("a32nx-mcdu").fsInstrument.legacyFms.guidanceController` — which exposes the same `alongTrackDistancesToDestination.get(0)`, the `(T/D)`/`(T/C)` pseudo-waypoint with `flightPlanInfo.distanceFromAircraft`/`secondsFromPresent`, and `A32NX_FMGC_FLIGHT_PHASE` as the A380. The A320 drives its MCDU over the **SimBridge relay** (NOT the Coherent MCDU bridge), so it can't reuse the A380's persistent `CoherentDebuggerClient`; instead `MainForm.AnnounceA32NXFlightInfo` runs a **ONE-SHOT** eval of the self-contained `Resources/coherent-a32nx-flightinfo.js` via the lightweight `SimConnect/CoherentEvalClient` (resolve the `A32NX_MCDU` view → eval → close, no agent/scrape-loop, zero A380 risk). `FlyByWireA320Definition.HandleHotkeyAction` routes `ReadDistanceToDest`/`ReadDistanceToTOD` there, and BOTH jets share the parse+announce (`MainForm.AnnounceFlightInfoJson`) so they read identically (PMDG-format TOD, phase-based "Past top of descent"). Live-verified `distToDest` on the A320; the TOD/time path uses the same pseudo-waypoint structure as the A380 (verify on an A320 descent). Destination ETA/EFOB still not included.

**MFD action auto-refresh (dropdowns / company-fpln insert).** `FBWA380MCDUForm` only re-fetched the page on navigation, never after a `click_mcdu_element`. So activating the company-fpln dropdown button opened its `INSERT*`/`CLEAR*` menu in the sim but the list never updated to show them — the action read as "nothing happened" (the user's "Enter didn't click"). `ScheduleRefresh()` (a 450 ms post-action re-fetch, mirroring the page-selector) now runs after every click, field-commit and clear, so dropdown menu items and page changes appear. Insertion path itself = "RECEIVED CPNY F-PLN" button (Enter) → menu appears → arrow to `INSERT*` → Enter.

**External-power / GSX announcement fix.** The GPU-available vars read the FBW L-var `A32NX_EXT_PWR_AVAIL:n`, whose name literally contains a colon index; the SimConnect data-definition path (`L:{Name}`) mis-parses `:n` as an index of a (nonexistent) base var, so the value was never read and GSX connecting ground power announced nothing. Switched to the **stock indexed simvar `EXTERNAL POWER AVAILABLE:n`** (`SimVarType.SimVar`) — natively indexed via data defs AND exactly what GSX / stock ground power set (verified live: `:1`=1 with GSX power). NOTE: the only other colon-indexed L-var in the def is `A32NX_AUTOTHRUST_TLA:n` (thrust-lever angle → detent); if that announce is ever found broken, it has the same root cause.

**Page navigation.** The MCDU window steps pages on Ctrl+Up = previous and Ctrl+Down = next (plus PageUp/PageDown), each announcing "Previous/Next page" + re-fetching the page (the new title also auto-announces). The MFD has one LINEAR page order (plus vertical scroll within a page) — no horizontal page axis — so Left/Right are NOT bound to paging. Plain arrows move the line cursor.

**KCCU keys reach the MFD ONLY via its own EventBus (key finding).** `Coherent.trigger("H:A32NX_KCCU_L_<KEY>")` and `SimVar.SetSimVarValue("H:…")` do NOT reach the MFD from the external debugger — verified live (even a PERF *navigation* key was ignored), which is why F-PLN scrolling and KCCU input silently did nothing. The MFD subscribes to `'hEvent'` on its **own msfs-sdk EventBus**, reachable at `document.querySelector('a380x-mfd').fsInstrument.bus` (the `<a380x-mfd>` custom element also exposes `fsInstrument.fmcService` and `mfdCaptRef`/`mfdFoRef`). `coherent-a380-agent.js` `A.fireKey` now publishes the KCCU H-event there via `A.mfdBus()` (`bus.pub('hEvent','A32NX_KCCU_L_<KEY>',true)`), Coherent/SimVar as fallback. This makes **every** KCCU key work — navigation, EXEC, and F-PLN line scroll. **F-PLN scrolling is solved:** KCCU UP/DOWN moves the window one waypoint, so `A.pageCommand` fires the scroll key 6× for a page; the MCDU window's Ctrl+Up/Down / PageUp/PageDown now walk the whole route (verified: DER22→BASUR→DER22). The EventBus is also the path to `fmcService` (`fmcService.master.flightPlanInterface.active.allLegs` = the leg list). A user-facing "whole route" reader from `allLegs` was prototyped then REMOVED — scrolling is preferred, and notably the DOM F-PLN scroll renders MORE than `allLegs` (the full approach/missed-approach fixes, e.g. DB520…OMDB30R…HOLDR, which `allLegs` collapses to "IMPED, ‹disco›, CF, OMDB30R"), so the scroll is the more complete view. **Scroll verified non-skipping:** paging the F-PLN (6 KCCU-DOWN per page) over a ~8-waypoint window leaves a ~2-waypoint overlap between consecutive windows, so the whole route reads in sequence with nothing skipped (checked window-by-window VCBI22→OMDB approach). **F-PLN paging flakiness fix:** `coherent-a380-agent.js` `fireKey` was firing each KCCU H-event TWICE (`Coherent.trigger` AND `SimVar.SetSimVarValue("H:…")`), so F-PLN page up/down double-scrolled / behaved erratically; it now fires ONCE (Coherent.trigger, with the SimVar write only as a headless-eval fallback). Verified live: one page-down scrolls the F-PLN by exactly one window (VCBI22→BASUR). Setting the **arrival** (STAR/approach) uses the destination waypoint's lateral revision — scroll the F-PLN to the OMDB line at the end, activate it, choose ARRIVAL → approach; the bottom DEST/OMDB summary buttons do NOT open the revision.

**flyPad non-dashboard pages + KCCU.** The column-first read order is scoped to the Dashboard (`A.isDashboard`) — it was the only side-by-side two-widget page. Other EFB pages (Performance TOD calc, Ground, etc.) are single-widget/single-column and read acceptably top-to-bottom; generalize the column split only if a specific page is reported jumbled (a blind global split would break single-column pages). KCCU: MSFSBA drives the MFD via DOM click + `keypress` (the reliable path per `coherent-a380-agent.js`), NOT KCCU H-event emulation — the KCCU keys (`A32NX_KCCU_L_*`) are the cockpit hardware path and are less reliable for an external tool; DOM input is equivalent or better, so "using the KCCU" is not required.

**Native-additions audit (2026-05).** Most high-value A380 native data is ALREADY surfaced: autobrake selected/armed mode + RTO + `A32NX_BTV_STATE` + brake temps 1-16 (def §brakes), FQMS gross weight/CG/FOB + pax + DEST-EFOB-below-min (System Display window + Status), RMP active/standby freqs + squawk, EWD memos/warnings (EWD agent). FMS PERF V-speeds are NOT L-vars on the A380 (only `A32NX_SPEEDS_MANAGED_SHORT_TERM_PFD`) → would need an MFD PERF-page scrape.

**ROW/ROP runway-overrun protection (landing/taxi safety) — ADDED.** `A32NX_ROW_ROP_WORD_1` and `A32NX_OANS_WORD_1` are plain (non-indexed) ARINC429 discrete L-vars, registered Continuous+IsAnnounced and decoded in `ProcessSimVarUpdate` with `Arinc429Word.BitValueOr` (1-based, SSM-gated — identical to the FBW PFD `AttitudeIndicatorWarnings`). Bits → call-outs: ROW_ROP_WORD_1 **12 = "Maximum braking" (ROP under autobrake)**, **13 = "Max braking" (manual-braking warning)**, **14 = "If wet, runway too short"**, **15 = "Runway too short"**; OANS_WORD_1 **11 = "Runway ahead"**. Announced on each bit's RISING edge (tracked in `_rowRopActive`), silent at baseline (verified live: ROW_ROP=`0x3_00000000` SSM-NormalOp value 0; OANS=0 → SSM invalid → fallback false). Honours the Ctrl+M mute. **⚠️ These words CANNOT be injection-tested (established 2026-06-12):** both have ACTIVE per-frame writers (Rust autobrakes / the ND instrument) that stomp an external write within ~1 frame, while MSFSBA's continuous batch samples at SIMCONNECT_PERIOD.SECOND — a one-frame pulse is ~3% likely to be sampled. NOT a real-world gap: genuine activations persist for seconds (ROW through the approach, ROP through the rollout, RWY AHEAD up to 30 s), so the 1 Hz sample catches them; the decode is the same Arinc429Word path as the live-proven PFD words. Real verification needs a live scenario. **General rule: before planning an injection test for an announced var, check whether it has a PER-FRAME writer (Rust systems / a rendering instrument) — if so, only vars the writer leaves alone (TCAS detail vars, most switches) are injectable.**

**BTV (Brake-To-Vacate) rollout distance call-outs — ADDED.** During the landing rollout MSFSBA speaks the distance to the selected runway exit and the runway remaining as they count down. `A32NX_OANS_BTV_REMAINING_DIST_TO_EXIT` and `A32NX_OANS_BTV_REMAINING_DIST_TO_RWY_END` are **ARINC429 metres** (that's why a raw `get_lvar` reads 4294967296 = 2^32 when unset — decode with `Arinc429Word.ValueOr` + `IsNormalOperation`, like the ROW/ROP words). Registered Continuous+IsAnnounced; decoded in `ProcessSimVarUpdate`, announced as each descends through fixed thresholds (exit: 1200/800/500/300/150 m; rwy-end: 900/600/300/150 m), once each, then reset between landings. Gated on the **BTV state** (`A32NX_BTV_STATE`, now `Mon` = auto-announces its transitions Armed/Rotation Optimised/Decel/End of Braking, and captured into `_btvState`): distance call-outs only fire while state is Rotation Optimised(2)/Decel(3), i.e. the actual braking rollout — so they cannot fire on approach or the ground. Phrases: "{N} meters to exit", "{N} meters runway remaining". Honours the Ctrl+M mute (entries "BTV Distance to Exit", "Runway Remaining", "Brake To Vacate"). Verified: vars exist + are ARINC429 (2^32 sentinel on the ground, BTV_STATE=0); **the rollout numbers/cadence need verifying on a real landing**. Other BTV vars available if wanted: DRY/WET/STOP_BAR_DISTANCE_ESTIMATED (plain metres), OANS_RWY_LENGTH/BTV_ROT (ARINC). KCCU note: `A32NX_KCCU_{L,R}_KBD_ON_OFF` verified = 0 in the powered cockpit (FBW defaults to touchscreen), so sighted players have the KCCU keyboard OFF — MSFSBA leaves it off to match (no cosmetic write).

**Thrust-lever startup-spam fix.** The detent announce (`ProcessSimVarUpdate`, `A32NX_AUTOTHRUST_TLA:n`) began with `_lastEngDetent`/`_lastAllDetent` = null, so first start read out "Thrust lever 1/2/3/4 Idle, All thrust levers Idle". A `_tlaBaselineDone` guard now records the baseline detents SILENTLY until all four levers have reported once; only real detent CHANGES after that announce.

**TCAS resolution-advisory GUIDANCE — spoken "what to fly", BOTH jets (2026-06-12; fixes the unindexed-vspeed bug).** During an RA, FBW publishes the fly-to/avoid V/S bands **only as the `:1`/`:2` INDEXED L:vars** `A32NX_TCAS_VSPEED_GREEN:1/:2` + `_RED:1/:2` (min/max; `TcasComputer.ts:1267-1271`, A380 `LegacyTcasComputer.ts:1281-1285`) — **the unindexed names are never written**, so the A380's old `Read("A32NX_TCAS_VSPEED_GREEN")` panel fields could never see an RA (always 0). Both defs now register the indexed vars (Continuous batch — the proven transport for colon-indexed L:vars, TLA:n precedent) plus the plain detail vars `A32NX_TCAS_RA_CORRECTIVE` / `RA_UP/DOWN_ADVISORY_STATUS` (UpDownAdvisoryStatus 0-5) / `RA_RATE_TO_MAINTAIN`, cache them silently in `ProcessSimVarUpdate`, and speak **one composed sentence** via `ComposeTcasRaGuidance` while `A32NX_TCAS_STATE == 2`: corrective → *"TCAS: Climb. Fly vertical speed plus 1500 to plus 2000 feet per minute."*; preventive → the do-not limits / rate to maintain. Announced (`AnnounceImmediate`) only when the sentence CHANGES (covers strengthening/reversal), reset on leaving RA; the generic state announce ("TCAS advisory: resolution advisory") still fires (queued — a detail-driven immediate may land first). Mute rides the `A32NX_TCAS_STATE` Ctrl+M entry for both. The A380 panel band fields are now the `:1` keys, rendered as the full band from the cached values in `TryGetDisplayOverride`. **⚠️ STALE-CACHE GUARD (2026-06-12 bug pass): the RA-onset compose is DEFERRED ~800 ms, never synchronous from the state edge.** FBW resets corrective + the V/S band L:vars only in TCAS **STBY** — NOT on clear-of-conflict (`TcasComputer.ts:1381`; upstream #10662 resets only the up/down advisory + rate) — so at the onset of RA #2 the cache can still hold RA #1's values and an immediate compose could speak the OPPOSITE sense ("Climb" for a Descend) before the fresh batch values land. The deferred timer covers the values-unchanged case (identical values = identical, still-correct sentence); details that DID change announce fresh from their own handlers. TA state (1) speaks only the generic "traffic advisory" — TAs carry no guidance and RAs are inhibited on the ground/low altitude by design (TA-on-ground live-verified 2026-06-12 with real traffic). **USER-CONFIRMED END-TO-END (2026-06-12, MSFSBA running, both jets injected):** detail-var injection + state 2 produced the spoken "TCAS: Climb. Maintain plus 1500 feet per minute" — and because the details were written BEFORE the state flip, the sentence could only have come from the deferred timer, proving the timer ticks (ProcessSimVarUpdate runs on a pumped UI thread). The A380 mirror block was exercised with the same sequence. **STILL PENDING:** the colon-indexed `:1/:2` band reads need a REAL airborne RA (injection can't write colon-indexed names — only FBW internals can; if the batch mis-parses them à la EXT_PWR_AVAIL:n, guidance degrades to the advisory-status/rate wording, which is exactly what the injected tests speak).

**Announcement-quality patterns (2026-05 quality pass).**
- **ARINC429 enum guard.** Some FBW discretes are written `write_arinc429`, so an announced enum var arrives as a huge SSM-encoded word (e.g. `A32NX_APU_LOW_FUEL_PRESSURE_FAULT` = 12884901888 = 0x3_00000000 = SSM NormalOp, payload 0) that matches no 0/1 entry → the generic announce printed "<label>: 12884901888". `ProcessSimVarUpdate` opens with a generic guard: any ANNOUNCED enum var (`_varCache` lookup, `IsAnnounced`, `ValueDescriptions.Count>0`) whose raw value is ARINC-large (`>= 2^32`) is decoded via `Arinc429Word.ValueOr(0)` to its 0/1 payload, announced via its `ValueDescriptions` ON CHANGE only (default prev=0 so the initial no-fault is silent), honouring the Ctrl+M mute, and returns true. Future-proof for every such discrete. (Announced ARINC NUMERICS — EIS baro, minimums — are handled by their own `MonNum` + custom decode, so they have no ValueDescriptions and skip this guard.)
- **Annunciators are NOT panel read-out fields.** `GetPanelDisplayVariables` ends with a filter that strips every ANNOUNCED 2-state enum var (faults + non-fault binary lights) from the display sets — a pilot navigates a panel to operate CONTROLS, not to scan "X Fault: Normal" rows. KEPT: numeric/analog read-outs, multi-state (3+) status (ADIRU/engine state, autobrake/BTV/FMA modes), and the intentionally-silent `ReadEnumQuiet` binaries (their only surface). The stripped annunciators still auto-announce on change and stay in the Ctrl+M monitor (which lists every `Continuous+IsAnnounced` var regardless of type, so SimVar-state combos like the engine masters/crossfeeds/doors are included).
- **No double-announce: annunciator L-var vs ECAM memo.** When a status has BOTH a PB-light L-var and an E/WD memo, the L-var is made `ReadEnumQuiet` and the memo (from the scrape) is the single call-out — e.g. `A32NX_OVHD_APU_START_PB_IS_AVAILABLE` was announced twice ("APU Available: Available" + "APU AVAIL") → now only the memo speaks.

**PFD memo + limitations (string SimVars, scrape-read).** FwsCore publishes the 3 PFD MEMO lines + 8 PFD LIMITATIONS lines as FBW **'string'** SimVars (`A32NX_PFD_MEMO_LINE_1..3` / `A32NX_PFD_LIMITATIONS_LINE_1..8`), NOT numeric codes — so MSFSBA's numeric SimConnect read returns 0 and never sees them. The E/WD scrape agent (`coherent-ewd-agent.js` `A.pfdLines()`) reads them as strings from the Coherent JS context (`SimVar.GetSimVarValue(..., 'string')`, FWC codes stripped), and `CoherentEWDClient` announces them on change with the same baseline + dedup as the memos (SET HOLD SPD, SPEED LIM, …). The **INOP SYS** and **SD STATUS** lists are EventBus/DOM-only (like the abnormal procedures — `inopSysAllPhasesKeys`/`limitationsAllPhasesKeys` are EventBus Subjects, not SimVars), so they would need a DOM scrape of the STATUS area to surface. Source-mining note: the OIT "FLT OPS" terminal is a second EFB-like app (login/flight-folder/charts) — redundant with the accessible flyPad EFB and shows "not available" without the avionics network, so not exposed; BAT/FCU/RMP display content is already covered by the SimVar path.

**ECAM E/WD monitoring — TWO paths (memos via SimVar, failures via DOM scrape).** The A380 FwsCore splits its output: MASTER WARNING/CAUTION + the MEMO columns are on L-vars, but the sensed abnormal/warning PROCEDURES (failure titles + ECAM action items) are published on an in-process **EventBus, NOT SimVars** — they exist only as rendered text in the `A380X_EWD` Coherent view's DOM. So there are two readout paths, deliberately non-overlapping:
- **Memos (SimVar path).** Upper E/WD memo lines `A32NX_EWD_LOWER_LEFT/RIGHT_LINE_1..10` (uppercase `EWD`, 10/side — vs A320's `Ewd`/7; both are MEMO columns) are numeric message CODES decoded via `SimConnect/EWDMessageLookupA380.cs` (1507-entry table: ported A380 `EcamMemos`/`EcamInfos`/`EcamLimitations`/`EcamInopSys` + abnormal titles; own ANSI stripper using fixed `` escapes) and announced live in `ProcessSimVarUpdate`. Dedup is per-SET via `_announcedEwdCodes` HashSet (kills scroll re-announce).
- **Failures (DOM scrape path).** `SimConnect/CoherentEWDClient.cs` is a **background monitor** (started on A380 load in MainForm, no window needed) that connects to the `A380X_EWD` Coherent view, installs `Resources/coherent-ewd-agent.js` (`window.__MSFSBA_EWD`, ES5), and polls `scrape()` once/sec. The agent reads each `.EclLine.AbnormalItem` row's **SVG-rendered tspans** (the clean text — the sibling `.EclLineText` span carries raw FWC codes `<4m`/`4m`/`m` and the checkbox holds `□`, so those are skipped). The C# client cleans each line (leader-dot runs → ", ", strip leading "-"), **filters the fixed ABN-PROC manual-procedure menu** (ABNORMAL PROC / SMOKE-FUMES / EMER EVAC / ENG / F/CTL / L/G / NAV / FUEL / MISCELLANEOUS / … — exact-match so "F/CTL PRIM 1 FAULT" ≠ the bare "F/CTL" menu entry), dedups by text, and **silently baselines on first scrape** (only failures appearing AFTER connect announce — matches every other MSFSBA monitor, avoids re-reading the whole screen on reconnect). Honours the Ctrl+M/Ctrl+E `FBWA380_ECAM_MEMOS` mute. The client ALSO announces the DOM `memos[]` (PARK BRK ON, ELEC EXT PWR, …) so the E/WD auto-call-outs come from ONE source — and while the scrape monitor runs, the SimVar `EWD_LOWER` memo auto-announce is suppressed (via the def's `EwdScrapeHandlesAnnounce` flag, set by `StartA380EWDMonitor`) to avoid double speech; the SimVar dedup sets are still maintained so the on-demand `ReadAllEwdWarnings` (Alt+E) decode works, and the flag defaults false so SimVar still announces if no scrape monitor is active. Live-verified end-to-end on a triggered PRIM 1 failure → announces "F/CTL PRIM 1 FAULT", "PRIM 1, OFF THEN ON", "IF NOT SUCCESSFUL :", "LDG DIST AFFECTED", and the FWS 1+2 & CPIOM FAULT items. The failure TITLES still in EWDMessageLookupA380 are dead weight for SimVar decoding (failures never appear as SimVar codes) — kept only as a code→text fallback.

**Live display DOM-scrape (SD / E/WD / ND / PFD / ISIS) — the generic readout core.** Every A380 cockpit display is a Coherent GT view with a DOM, so the crew-visible DECODED text (oxygen PSI, GW/FOB, per-tank fuel, N1/EGT, temps, pressures, doors, FMA, baro, …) can be read directly — which beats the SimVar path for TEXT-based displays (it needs no ARINC429 decode and catches values the SimVar set never modelled). Scrapability splits cleanly: **text displays win** (SD decoded values, E/WD, MCDU, flyPad); **graphical tape displays** (PFD/ND/ISIS current airspeed/altitude/attitude) are POSITIONAL so a flat scrape returns scale tick-marks, not readings — their SimVar windows stay primary there. Core pieces:
- `Resources/coherent-display-agent.js` (`window.__MSFSBA_DISP`, ES5) — GENERIC row reconstruction: collect leaf text elements (skip ones with element children), cluster by Y (±12 px), sort each cluster by X, join with spacing → readable rows exactly as a sighted pilot reads the screen. De-dups stacked outline+fill glyph copies. Works on any display view.
- `SimConnect/CoherentDisplayClient.cs` — GENERIC, title-needle-parameterised reader; installs the agent, polls `scrape()`, raises `RowsUpdated` only on change; `SetActive(false)` pauses polling when no window is open; `ScrapeNowAsync()` for F5.
- **SD reading — the live scrape** (the standalone `FBWA380SystemDisplayForm` window + its `ShowStatusPage`/`ShowECAM` hotkeys were REMOVED; the page selector now lives on the **ECAM Control Panel** "System Display Page" combo in the Pedestal panels): the selector drives `A32NX_ECAM_SD_CURRENT_PAGE_INDEX` (verified writable — index map from `SD/SystemDisplay.tsx`: 0 ENG,1 APU,2 BLEED,3 COND,4 PRESS,5 DOOR,6 ELEC-AC,7 ELEC-DC,8 FUEL,9 WHEEL,10 HYD,11 F/CTL,12 C/B,15 VIDEO,-1 default) so the user reads ANY page decoded — including Door/Wheel/F-CTL/C-B/Video the old ARINC429 decode never covered. The legacy SimVar+ARINC429 render is an automatic fallback when the SD view is unreachable.
- **`FBWA380LiveDisplayForm`** — generic live-scrape window for the rest: E/WD (`ReadDisplayUpperECAM`/Alt+E also opens it — engine N1/EGT/FF + memos + warnings), and ND/ISIS ("&Live scrape" button + **F6**) and PFD (shared `PFDForm`, **F6** gated to `AircraftCode=="FBW_A380"`, no visible button so the A320 is unaffected). For the tape displays this AUGMENTS the SimVar window (positional values read as ticks).

**Monitor Manager (Ctrl+M) + ECAM toggle (Ctrl+E).** `FBWA380MonitorManagerForm` dynamically lists every auto-announced var (Continuous + IsAnnounced) with checkboxes, persisting un-ticked keys to `UserSettings.A380DisabledMonitorVariables` (consulted in `MainForm.OnSimVarUpdated`; the synthetic `FBWA380_ECAM_MEMOS` key mutes ECAM call-outs in `ProcessSimVarUpdate`). `HotkeyAction.ToggleECAMMonitoring` (Ctrl+E) flips that sentinel directly. **Annunciators auto-announce:** overhead pushbutton FAULT lights and system warnings are `ReadEnum`/`Mon` (Continuous+IsAnnounced) so they speak on change and the user can mute any in Ctrl+M — covers HYD per-engine A/B + electric-pump faults, ELEC emer-gen-line, COND ram-air + TADD, and the APU EGT / thrust-lever / performance / TCAS warnings (var names from the FBW A380 source). Mirrors the Fenix/PMDG monitor managers. The framework auto-monitor, read-only per-panel display fields, and combo auto-update-on-change are all free (driven off `GetVariables`/`GetPanelDisplayVariables`).

**Most names are verified against FBW docs/source, not the running sim** — but a chunk has now been live-verified: FCU set/readback + SI conversions, V/S sign, managed-mode dot, EFIS baro decode/STD/QNH/unit + `KOHLSMAN_SET`, minimums decode, the #59 FCU toggle events (AP1/AP2/LOC/APPR/EXPED = `A32NX.FCU_*_PUSH`; A/THR = stock `AUTO_THROTTLE_ARM`, NOT a dot-event; TRK/FPA = direct L-var write, no event; SPD/MACH = `A32NX.FCU_SPD_MACH_TOGGLE_PUSH`), all EFIS-CP controls via the MobiFlight calculator path (`ExecuteCalculatorCode("{val} (>L:{key})")` — `SetLVar`/data-def write is unreliable for FBW L-vars), thrust-lever detents, reversers (inboard 2/3 only), and that the FD is uncontrollable. Still flagged uncertain / need an in-sim pass: SURV pushbuttons, RMP per-channel TX, wing/pitot anti-ice write path (#56). Hotkey guide: `HotkeyGuides/FBW_A380_Hotkeys.txt`.

**#103 BREAKTHROUGH — the "computed-output PBs revert" conclusion was WRONG; ALL overhead pushbuttons are settable (live Coherent + calculator-path write-then-readback, 2026-05).** `HandleUIVariableSet` ends with a catch-all that routes every settable `A32NX_OVHD_*` / `A380X_OVHD_*` / `A32NX_KNOB_OVHD_*` / **`XMLVAR_*`** combo through the MobiFlight calculator path (`ExecuteCalculatorCode("{int} (>L:{key})")`) instead of MainForm's generic data-def `SetLVar`. **The earlier #60 verdict that PACK 1-2, HOT AIR 1-2, ENGINE 1-4 BLEED, CABIN/AIR-EXTRACT FANS, the HYD ENGINE/ELEC PUMP PBs, ELEC BUS-TIE/GALLEY, HYD PTU and the EMERGENCY-EXIT sign are "computed outputs that revert and cannot be set externally" was an ARTIFACT of testing with the MCP's native data-def write (`set_lvar` / `AddToDataDefinition` / `SetDataOnSimObject`), which is unreliable for FBW L:vars — exactly as the data-def READS are.** Re-tested live with the CALCULATOR path (`{val} (>L:{var})`, the one MSFSBA actually uses): EVERY one STICKS in both directions for 3+ s (pack set OFF stayed OFF; bus-tie/galley/PTU/HYD-eng-pumps/HYD-elec-pumps/eng-bleeds/cabin-fans/air-extract/hot-air all stuck; the EMEREXIT XMLVAR stuck). Source confirms why: the Rust `OnOffFaultPushButton` **READS** `{name}_PB_IS_ON/_IS_AUTO` as the pilot input every frame and only **WRITES** the `_HAS_FAULT` output — so an external set to the IS_ON/IS_AUTO var IS the button press (the `write_by_name("..._PB_IS_ON")` calls in `air_conditioning/mod.rs` are in `#[cfg(test)]` harness code, not the controller). **So all these overhead combos actuate correctly through the calculator path — there is NO hard FBW limitation.** These were already registered as settable combos (`OnOff`/`OffAuto`/`Sel`) and already routed through the OVHD calculator catch-all, so the OVHD ones worked already; the only real gap was the **`XMLVAR_` sign combos** (No Smoking, Emergency Exit, Altitude Increment) which fell through to the unreliable data-def path — **now routed through the calculator path too** (added `XMLVAR_` to the catch-all). **General lesson: to test whether an FBW L:var write sticks, ALWAYS use the calculator path (`(>L:VAR)` via `execute_calculator_code` or Coherent `SimVar.SetSimVarValue`), NEVER the data-def `set_lvar` — the latter silently fails for many FBW vars and produces false "reverts/uncontrollable" conclusions.** The only PBs that genuinely need a stock event are the seatbelt sign (`CABIN_SEATBELTS_ALERT_SWITCH_TOGGLE`, handled earlier) and engine anti-ice (`ANTI_ICE_SET_ENGn`).
- **Writable single-writer PBs (always worked):** COMMERCIAL, IDG disconnect, EXT PWR, battery selector, all FUEL transfer + jettison PBs, DITCHING, RAM AIR, APU BLEED, lighting selectors.

Other #60 findings:
- **Non-OVHD FBW settable L-vars are writable** via the calculator path — verified live for SURV (`A32NX_SWITCH_RADAR_PWS_Position`, `A32NX_RADAR_MULTISCAN_AUTO`, `A32NX_RADAR_GCS_AUTO`), GPWS (`A32NX_GPWS_*_OFF`), and the source-switching knobs (`A32NX_FMS_SWITCHING_KNOB`, `A32NX_ATT_HDG_SWITCHING_KNOB`, …). These still go through MainForm's generic data-def `SetLVar` (not the catch-all, which is OVHD-only) and that works for them — left as-is to avoid touching the many controls currently functioning.
- **Fuel crossfeed was broken → fixed.** The four XFEED combos wrote `XMLVAR_Momentary_PUSH_OVHD_FUEL_XFEED{n}_Pressed`, which is only the cockpit model's press-animation flag and never actuates the valve (verified: pulsing it left `FUELSYSTEM VALVE SWITCH:n` unchanged). The FBW `FBW_Airbus_Fuel_Crossfeed` template drives `#ID# (>K:FUELSYSTEM_VALVE_TOGGLE)` with valve IDs **46-49**. Now a single **Closed/Open combo** per valve (state = SimVar `FUELSYSTEM VALVE SWITCH:id`, set fires `FUELSYSTEM_VALVE_OPEN`/`_CLOSE` via `HandleUIVariableSet`). OPEN/CLOSE (not TOGGLE) because TOGGLE was observed to stick mid-transition. NOTE: the MCP's `trigger_event` does not know the `FUELSYSTEM_VALVE_*` family ("not found"), but MSFSBA's `SendEvent` (`MapClientEventToSimEvent` + `TransmitClientEvent`) maps them by raw name and they work — proven by the engine masters. The momentary-button rule generalises: **a `_PRESSED`/`_Pressed` XMLVAR is almost always a model-only animation flag, not the actuator** — find the real K-event or state var instead of pulsing it.

**ECAM-CP and momentary/test controls are now BUTTONS (user request 2026-06, reversing the all-combo rule for these).** The `Btn` and `PressSilent` helpers render `RenderAsButton = true` and route the click through the `_momentaryButtons` path (pulse the L:var 1→0, speak "<name> pressed") — so every A380 ECAM-CP key (ALL/ABNPROC/CL/CLR/CLR2/RCL/TOCONFIG/EMERCANC/UP/DOWN/MORE/CHECK_LH/CHECK_RH) plus the chronometer Start-Stop / Reset is a push-button. HOLD tests (Fire Test, the new **Cargo Smoke Detection Test** `A32NX_FIRE_TEST_CARGO`) use a new `ToggleBtn` helper (`_toggleButtons`): the click reads the current state, writes the opposite via the calculator path, and announces the new On/Off. The **System Display Page selector stays a combo** (it's a real selector, not a button). Mirror this on the A32NX (its ECAM keys are HVar PressEvent/ReleaseEvent — a different mechanism, convert with care). Fenix is the template: it renders ECAM-CP controls as `RenderAsButton` L:var buttons (optionally with a `StateVariable` indicator) and the generic MainForm button path fires + announces.

**Generic ARINC429 auto-decoder.** `SimVarDefinition` has `IsArinc429` + `Arinc429Unit`/`Arinc429Format`/`Arinc429NotAvailableText`; `BaseAircraftDefinition.TryDecodeArinc429(varKey, value, out text)` decodes any flagged var via `Arinc429Word` ("<value> <unit>" on NormalOp/FuncTest, else not-available). Hooked in `MainForm.UpdateDisplayText` (after `TryGetDisplayOverride`, so ad-hoc baro/minimums/rudder decoders still win) and the announce path (only for vars `ProcessSimVarUpdate` didn't handle, so no double-decode). Flag any new ARINC var (BTV distances, FQMS/PRESS percentage words) `IsArinc429 = true` and it surfaces decoded on panels + announce instead of a raw ~14-billion word — no per-var case needed.

**Display-value fixes (2026-06, audit + live-verified via `get_lvar`).** Four A380 fields were reading wrong/raw values; all fixed and confirmed against the live L:vars:
- **Engine Fuel Used** — was the stock `GENERAL ENG FUEL USED SINCE START:n` (reads **0** on the FBW A380; the stock engine model isn't driving it). Now reads the FBW L:var **`A32NX_FUEL_USED:n`** (kg) — the same var the SD ENGINE page uses (live: `A32NX_FUEL_USED:1` = 17.4 kg while the stock var read 0). Key stays `ENG_FUEL_USED:n`, `Type=LVar, OnRequest`.
- **V-speeds (V1/VR/V2)** — were stock `AIRLINER V1/VR/V2 SPEED` (not populated). Now read FBW L:vars **`AIRLINER_V1/VR/V2_SPEED`** (knots) — written by the MFD PERF page (10/7/6 occurrences in FBW source). Keys stay `PFD_V1/VR/V2`.
- **APU Fuel Used** — was a plain kg read of `A32NX_APU_FUEL_USED`, which is actually an **ARINC429** word (`useArinc429Var` in FBW source → raw ~13.9-billion). Now flagged `IsArinc429=true` (`Arinc429Unit="kg"`) so it decodes to a small kg value.
- **APU Low Fuel Pressure** — `A32NX_APU_LOW_FUEL_PRESSURE_FAULT` is an ARINC429 **enum** word (raw 12884901888 = SSM NormalOp + payload 0). Added a **generic ARINC-enum display decode** in `MainForm.UpdateDisplayText` (after `TryDecodeArinc429`, before the `ValueDescriptions` branch): when a var has `ValueDescriptions` and `value >= 2^32`, decode the ARINC payload and look it up in `ValueDescriptions` → "Normal". This auto-handles **any** ARINC-enum status field (no per-var case), distinct from the `IsArinc429` numeric path.

**Display-value fixes pass 2 (2026-06, full live in-cruise audit of all 16 SD pages + panels).** Three more spurious-0 readouts found and live-verified via `get_lvar`:
- **Passengers on Board** (Status panel) — the field read `A32NX_FMS_PAX_NUMBER`, which is written **only** by the MFD FUEL&LOAD page (`MfdFmsFuelLoad.tsx`); boarding via the flyPad never sets it, so it read 0 (live-confirmed 0 with a full cabin). Fixed: `FlyByWireA380Definition` registers the 14 per-station seat-bitmask L:vars (`A32NX_PAX_MAIN_FWD_A` … `A32NX_PAX_UPPER_AFT`) as **Continuous + IsAnnounced + ExcludeFromMonitorManager** (live-cached, never spoken, not in Ctrl+M), `ProcessSimVarUpdate` **popcounts each** (`BitOperations.PopCount((ulong)(long)value)` — each station ≤ 50 seats so the integer bitmask is < 2^53 and exact as a double, exactly how the FBW EFB reads them) and keeps a running `_paxOnBoard`, and `TryGetDisplayOverride("A32NX_FMS_PAX_NUMBER")` returns that total. So the Status field shows the **real boarded count** (sum of occupied seats), matching the flyPad. Field relabeled "Passengers on Board".
- **AC EHA bus / DC EHA bus** (ELEC AC + DC SD pages) — read the **invented** vars `A32NX_ELEC_AC_EHA_BUS_IS_POWERED` / `_DC_EHA_BUS_IS_POWERED`, which don't exist (always 0 → "not powered" when they ARE powered in flight). The A380 electro-hydrostatic-actuator backup buses are the **named buses 247XP (AC) / 247PP (DC)**, which publish under the **bare name** (`shared/mod.rs`: `AlternatingCurrentNamed(name) => write!("{}", name)`), so the real vars are `A32NX_ELEC_247XP_BUS_IS_POWERED` / `A32NX_ELEC_247PP_BUS_IS_POWERED` (live-verified = powered). Same "invented string-named ELEC var" trap as the `BAT_ESS/APU_POTENTIAL` note in the ELEC-DC SD rows. **General rule: FBW named AC/DC buses (and batteries) publish `A32NX_ELEC_{rawName}_BUS_IS_POWERED` with the raw bus id (247XP, 247PP, 309PP, AC_ESS_SHED, …) — never invent a descriptive `_AC_EHA_`/`_DC_EHA_` name; confirm the id in `alternating_current.rs`/`direct_current.rs`.**
- **Audit also confirmed two NON-bugs** (don't "fix" them): the Cockpit-duct-temp readout (`A32NX_COND_CKPT_DUCT_TEMP`) reads a real ~41 °C live (it exists); and the brake temps — `A32NX_BRAKE_TEMPERATURE_n` is the raw physics temp (live -60 °C cold-soaked at altitude) while `A32NX_REPORTED_BRAKE_TEMPERATURE_n` is the BTMU value the real WHEEL SD page shows (0 when cold, real when hot, `Wheel.tsx:21`). MSFSBA's WHEEL SD page already uses REPORTED (cockpit-matching); the Autobrake panel uses the raw temp. Both are legitimate — neither is a spurious 0.

**Pushback: NEVER implement the FBW flyPad pushback** (heading/speed factor L:vars) — Robin's team uses GSX for pushback (much better); permanent decision 2026-06-11.

**Ground services + calls (A380).** The cabin/mechanic Calls push-buttons (`PUSH_OVHD_CALLS_ALL/FWD/AFT/MECH`) are panel controls. (Earlier `A380X_GND_*` truck "Activate" combos firing `REQUEST_FUEL_KEY`/`REQUEST_LUGGAGE`/`REQUEST_CATERING` were NEVER added to the A380 def — the trucks are requested on the flyPad Ground page, and MSFSBA auto-announces their connection via the door monitor — see the "Ground-service AUTO-ANNOUNCE" note below. The only `A380X_GND_*` vars are chocks/cones/GPU-avail.)

**Surveillance panel + transponder/TCAS for VATSIM — the verdict (2026-06, FBW docs + live).** FBW's own docs state the **pedestal Surveillance panel is "not yet fully implemented" in the A380X** — so there is NOTHING to make accessible there (it doesn't exist as a working panel), and the **Weather Radar is inoperative**. ALL XPDR/TCAS/TAWS/WXR setup is done on the **MFD SURV CONTROLS page** (`surv/controls`, already in `AllPages` → reachable via the MCDU window's page picker; clickable radio buttons, live-verified). When FBW ships the pedestal panel, add it then. **Transponder IS genuinely AUTO-managed (a real A380 thing FBW models):** you set the SQWK code + click **AUTO** on the MFD SURV page; AUTO auto-selects the reply mode (Standby/Mode C) by air/ground state. The stock `TRANSPONDER STATE:1` (what vPilot/swift read on VATSIM) is what it drives, so it Just Works — STBY on ground, Mode C airborne (live-verified the systems-host holds STBY on ground and reverts any external write). **For TAXI you set the TRANSPONDER (XPDR AUTO + squawk), NOT the TCAS** — TCAS TA/RA is the in-flight traffic system, separate from the transponder ATC sees. MSFSBA surfaces the result as the read-only auto-announcing "Transponder Mode" (so the pilot hears "Mode C" on departure). **Flight-deck API sweep** (docs.flybywiresim.com/aircraft/a380x/a380x-api): the documented settable LVARs are all already exposed by MSFSBA (autopilot, baro, ND range, ADIRS, elec, packs, temp selectors, hydraulics, flaps/spoilers/gear/parkbrake/autobrake, lighting presets) — no transponder/TCAS settable var exists (confirms EventBus-only). **Cockpit-prep INOP list (do NOT expose as working):** RECORDER GROUND CTL, EVAC, ELT, BODY ACCUMULATOR PRESSURE, COCKPIT DOOR SWITCH, CVR TEST, OXYGEN MASKS TEST.

**Ground-service AUTO-ANNOUNCE when called via the flyPad (2026-06).** The flyPad Ground page drives every A380 service through the stock SimVar **`INTERACTIVE POINT OPEN:n`** (source: `fbw-common/.../EFB/Ground/Pages/Services/A380_842/A380Services.tsx`): cabin doors 0/2/9/10 (jet-bridge/stairs/catering attach to these), GPU = `A32NX_EXT_PWR_AVAIL:1-4`, **front cargo hatch (baggage truck) = point 16**, **fuelling (fuel truck) = point 18**. MSFSBA's door monitor (`_doorDefs`) covered points 0-15 + the 2 cargo-LOCKED L:vars, so a flyPad **baggage** or **fuel** call went UNannounced (the cabin-door/GPU services already announce via their doors / EXT PWR). Fix: added points 16 + 18 to `_doorDefs` (`A380X_MSFSBA_DOOR_16` "Front Cargo Door (Baggage)", `A380X_MSFSBA_DOOR_18` "Fuel Truck") so they ride the proven once-per-transition door announce (Continuous+IsAnnounced, `_doorOpen` edge-detect). The fuel-truck point (18) speaks **connected/disconnected** (special-cased verb in the door-announce branch); the cargo hatch keeps open/closed; both also show in the Doors status window. Live-verified both are valid readable SimVars (0.0 = closed on the ground). The trucks have NO separate "connection" var beyond their interactive point — these ARE the readable states; catering/stairs/jet-bridge have no point of their own (they reuse the cabin doors), so labelling them as distinct services isn't possible without a GSX dependency.

**RMP = a dedicated SCRAPED WINDOW (`Ctrl+Shift+R` input mode → `Forms/FBWA380/FBWA380RmpForm`), NOT a control panel.** The old per-key RMP button panel was impractical (one digit at a time) and was REMOVED (registrations, `p["Radio Management Panel"]` + its structure entry, the `A380X_MSFSBA_RMP1_` HandleUIVariableSet branch, the `_SET` freq field). The window scrapes the live `A380X_RMP_1` (Captain) / `A380X_RMP_2` (First Officer) Coherent views via `CoherentDisplayClient` + **`Resources/coherent-rmp-agent.js`** (a new ES5 agent that registers as `window.__MSFSBA_DISP` — same `{ok,rows}` contract as the generic display agent, so `CoherentDisplayClient` reads it unchanged; the client gained an optional `agentFileName` ctor param). The agent zips the flat `.active-frequency` / `.transceiver-ident` / `.stby-frequency-cell` rows by index and reads the `.stby-frequency` div's `textContent` (which concatenates its 6 digit children + dot into "121.950" — and shows the live SCRATCHPAD while typing), with `reverse-video`=transmit, `.selected`=the keyed row. **Live-verified both RMP_1 and RMP_2 scrape clean rows** ("VHF1: active 122.800, standby 121.950, transmit, selected" / VHF2/3 / message line). The window: a **Captain / First Officer / Overhead combo (RMP 1/2/3)** (re-points the scrape view `A380X_RMP_{n}` + the keypad H-event index `RMP_{n}_*`; the overhead RMP 3 was added 2026-06 — `A380X_RMP_3` view confirmed live + agent installs + `RMP_3_*` H-events accepted, structurally identical to the verified RMP 1/2; the `SendRmpKey*` guard was widened from `1|2` to `1..3`), a read-only multiline TextBox you read with the arrow keys AND type the digits into (no separate field — see below; the FBW RMP AUTO-COMPLETES — `8`→118.000, `11850`→118.500 — so the decimal is stripped, per `VhfComController.onDigitEntered`), and page buttons (VHF / Transponder) in the tab order; all soft keys are keyboard shortcuts firing the real cockpit keypad H-events. **Write path live-verified:** firing `(>H:RMP_1_DIGIT_8_PRESSED/RELEASED)` via the calculator path types into the standby scratchpad (the `KeypadController` only acts when the EventBus `RmpState` is On — which it IS even though the legacy L:var `A32NX_RMP_1_STATE` reads 0; ignore that var). Def helper: `SendRmpKey(rmp, key, …)` (a single keypad key, press+release) plus `SendRmpKeyPress`/`SendRmpKeyRelease` for the held full-clear, parameterised for RMP 1/2/3. (The old batched `SendRmpKeypad(text, …)` was removed — digits are keyed one at a time as the user types.) The **active VHF freq auto-announces on change** (`FBW_RMP_FREQUENCY_ACTIVE_n` → `MonNum` + a `ProcessSimVarUpdate` branch that formats raw-Hz→MHz, range-gated to 118–137 so the uninitialised ~19 MHz value while unpowered is cached silently; standby stays an on-request readout, so no duplicate). Source: `fbw-a380x/.../instruments/src/RMP/` (`KeypadController`, `VhfComPage`/`VhfComController`). The window is a **live region**: `FBWA380RmpForm.AnnounceChanges` speaks the SELECTED row's standby when it auto-completes/changes ("Standby 118.000") + any new RMP message, on every scrape change (silent on the first scrape / side switch); the active freq is intentionally NOT spoken here (the global active-announce owns it — no dup). **The old "Radios" panel (stock COM standby-set + swap) was REMOVED** — live-verified the FBW A380 IGNORES the stock `COM_STBY_RADIO_SET_HZ` / `COM*_RADIO_SWAP` events (set COM1 standby to 119.000 → stayed 121.95); all tuning is RMP-only, so the stock panel was dead. The read-only **"RMP" panel** (3 state readouts + the `FBW_RMP_FREQUENCY_*` active/standby freq box, `d["RMP"]`) is KEPT as a quick-glance in the panel list (the window is the interactive interface). **UI is MODELLED ON THE ACCESSIBLE MCDU/CDU FORMS (decluttered, keyboard-driven).** The display is a read-only multiline **TextBox** (the RMP touchscreen IS text), Consolas, focused on open, caret-preserved across refreshes. NO action buttons — every soft key is a keyboard shortcut using the SAME scheme as `FlyByWireMCDUForm`/`FenixMCDUForm`/`PMDG777CDUForm` (left=Ctrl, right=Alt, honouring the shared `MCDUUseAlternateLSKKeys` setting): **Ctrl+1/2/3 = `LSK_1/2/3`** (the left line keys — select the radio, or load the standby if already selected); **Alt+1/2/3 = `ADK_1/2/3`** (the right keys — swap active↔standby, MANUAL, never auto); F1/2/3 + F7/8/9 in alternate mode. Pages **Alt+V** (VHF) / **Alt+Q** (transponder — the only two the FBW build models) + buttons in the tab order; **Alt+C** = full clear; **Alt+Home** = focus the screen. (The VHF3 standby-mode cycler — keypad `UP`/`DOWN` → `vhf_com_set_standby_mode_3` — was wired but **live-verified to have NO observable effect in the FBW dev build** — the publish doesn't round-trip to `vhf_com_standby_mode_3` — so the `Alt+Up/Down` keys were removed; the agent still surfaces a `standby emergency` suffix from `.stdby-mode`=EMER if the mode is ever set elsewhere.) **There is NO separate entry field — you TYPE the digits on the read-only display itself** (`_display.KeyPress`→`SendRmpKey DIGIT_n` keyed live; the box is read-only so the digits go to the radio, not the text; Backspace→one `DIGIT_CLR`; no decimal — the RMP auto-completes), **Enter** (`_display.KeyDown`) = `LSK_{selectedRow}` (load standby). Arrow keys still read the screen. **Announce-on-change mirrors the MCDU scratchpad**: a 300 ms debounce timer speaks the selected radio's `Standby <freq>` when it changes AND any new RMP **message** (e.g. "VHF FREQ NOT VALID") — via `_announcer.Announce` (queued), silent on the first scrape. Two FBW gotchas remain the reason the flow needs care: (1) `onDigitEntered` early-returns while the entry is invalid, so a stuck bad entry blocks all digits — **Alt+C** HOLDS CLR past the FBW 1 s timer (`SendRmpKeyPress`/`SendRmpKeyRelease "DIGIT_CLR"`, 1150 ms) for a full clear; (2) typing only builds a scratchpad — Enter LOADs (LSK), swap is separate (ADK). 500 ms auto-poll; `RaiseRows` marshals to the UI thread via `_syncContext` (same as the working E/WD window). **Repeated-key entry needs the anti-dedup seq prefix (2026-06-13).** `SendRmpKey` fires `{++_rmpKeySeq} 0 * (>H:RMP_n_KEY_PRESSED) (>H:RMP_n_KEY_RELEASED)` — the leading `{seq} 0 *` (same idiom as `FireDcduEvent` / the seat-motor ticks) makes every call's calc string textually UNIQUE, because MobiFlight's command channel COALESCES two consecutive identical strings. Without it, typing a doubled digit (the "22" in 122.800, the "00" in 122.800) silently dropped the second press → **122.800 became 128.000** (the dropped-duplicate `12800` auto-completes to `128.000`), and a select-then-load double-press of the SAME `LSK_n` / swap double-press of `ADK_n` no-op'd the second press. The earlier "verified" repeats `118500`/`11850` HID the bug because their auto-complete pads the dropped-duplicate result (`1850`) back to the correct `118.500` — `122.800` is the case that exposes it. Both press+release stay in the ONE calc call (CRITICAL #1 above) so the same-frame-overwrite fix is preserved. (`ADK_1` swaps active — verified.) NOTE: the A380 MCDU is cursor-driven (no LSK), so the RMP keyboard model is copied from the A320/PMDG CDU forms, not the A380 MFD — the RMP uses its own keypad H-events. **PAGES — the FBW A380 RMP dev build models exactly TWO** (`RmpPageStack` routes only `VhfPage`/`SquawkPage`): **VHF** (the 3 transceivers) and **Transponder/SQWK** (mode AUTO/STBY + squawk code + IDENT). HF/TEL/NAV/MENU do NOTHING (the page keys are dropped) — so the window offers only **VHF + Transponder** as buttons (in the tab order) + Alt+V/Alt+Q; the dead keys were removed. The page selectors are live-verified both directions on Captain AND First Officer. The agent was page-aware-fixed: the hidden page's rows still exist in the DOM (display:none, rect 0×0), so the transceiver loop now **skips rows where `!vis(actives[i])`** and the transponder reader keys on `.transponder-mode`/`.transponder-code .cyan`/`.transponder-ident` — otherwise the SQWK page read the hidden VHF rows (and vice-versa). SQWK-page actions route the same keys differently (the RMP routes page keys to the active page): digits = squawk entry, Enter (`LSK`) = `onValidate`, Alt+3 (`ADK_3`) = `onIdentPressed`; source `TransponderPage.tsx`/`TransponderController.ts`.

**RMP REDESIGN (2026-06 — SUPERSEDES the scrape-standby + SQWK-keypad description above; user-verified working).** After many live iterations the window (`FBWA380RmpForm`) was reworked so NO readback depends on a racy scrape. The scrape is still used for the freq DISPLAY + the message line, but never for the spoken readback. Key changes:
- **Unified page-mode screen.** One read-only screen TextBox for both pages; **`Alt+V`** = VHF page, **`Alt+T`** = Transponder page (these also drive the cockpit RMP to the matching page, best-effort). The page buttons have NO mnemonic — `Alt+V`/`Alt+T` are handled in `OnFormKeyDown` so they can't steal focus onto a button. The standalone "Squawk" field was removed (the unified screen does both).
- **VHF readback is computed from the TYPED digits, NOT the scrape.** The FBW autocomplete settles over SEVERAL FRAMES after the last keystroke (`VhfComController.onDigitEntered`: a completed entry = `entered.padEnd(6,'0')` shown `XXX.XXX`), so a single/polled scrape catches a transient (`123`→123.000 while the final is 123.500 — the user's bug). The form now remembers the typed digits (`_vhfEntry`) and formats the readback with that exact rule (`FormatVhfEntry`): `123500` and `1235` both → "VHF standby N, 123.500"; `12345`→123.450. Falls back to a scrape-settle read only for the rare leading-omitted shortcut (`8`=118.000) that doesn't form a 118–137 MHz value. Announced on the typing-settle debounce (~350 ms) and FORCED on Enter / re-press of the selected radio.
- **Row selection is authoritative from `Ctrl+1/2/3`; the scrape syncs `_selectedRowIndex` ONLY on the first scrape (init).** FBW rule (`VhfComPage` onLineSelectKey/onAdkKey): an LSK/ADK on a NON-selected row only SELECTS it; a SECOND press on the already-selected row loads (LSK) / swaps (ADK). A per-poll `_selectedRowIndex` sync RACED the LSK-select registration lag and reset a fresh VHF2/3 selection back to row 0 (symptom: "says VHF standby 1, won't swap"; VHF1 worked only because it's the default selected row). Now it's synced once then driven by `Ctrl+N`, and the form's own LSK presses keep the cockpit in sync.
- **Squawk via the stock `XPNDR_SET` event — RMP-page-INDEPENDENT.** The page-switch + keypad + auto-validate chain was unreliable to drive from the app (the squawk silently never set). On the SQWK page typed digits build a 4-digit (0–7) code committed on the 4th digit (or Enter) by **`def.SetSquawkFromForm`** = `0x{code} (>K:XPNDR_SET)` (live-verified to set `TRANSPONDER CODE:1` regardless of RMP page). It speaks "Squawk NNNN" once and primes the `XPNDR_CODE` monitor (`_formSetSquawkBcd`) to skip its duplicate (no race: the monitor matches the VALUE, not a timestamp). **IDENT = `Alt+I`** → `def.SendTransponderIdent` = `(>K:XPNDR_IDENT_ON)`.
- **Transponder mode readout is EXACT** — `XPNDR_STATE` enum verified against FBW `RMP/Data/TransponderPublisher.ts` + `MFD/SURV`: **0 Off · 1 Standby · 2 Test · 3 Mode A · 4 Mode C · 5 Mode S**. Mode S (5) on the ground in AUTO is CORRECT, not a bug (an earlier decode mislabelled 5 as "Mode C"). The squawk line is built from the reliable stock simvars (`XPNDR_CODE` BCO16 decode + `XPNDR_STATE`).
- **Live region = announce DIRECTLY in `Apply`, no debounce timer.** The old 300 ms standby/message debounce-timer announce was RESET by the 300 ms scrape poll every cycle, so it never ticked (that was "autocomplete never announced"). The message line now announces directly in `Apply` (deduped). The per-keystroke standby announce was REMOVED entirely (chatty) — only the LOADED value is read back.
- **`Apply` marshals to the UI thread** (`if (InvokeRequired) BeginInvoke`): the async `ScrapeNowAsync` continuation can resume OFF the UI thread, where `_announcer.Announce` silently fails AND the dedup key still updates (so the next UI-thread poll then sees "no change") — that masked the readbacks. The squawk/Enter announces always worked because they fire synchronously on the UI thread.
- Side combo **Captain / First Officer / Overhead** (RMP 1/2/3) unchanged. The coherent-rmp-agent scrape, the `SendRmpKey`/`SendRmpKeyPress`/`SendRmpKeyRelease` helpers, and the held-clear (`Alt+C`) are unchanged. **`Alt+C` no longer collides with a `&Close` button mnemonic** (button mnemonics were removed; Escape/Tab still close).

**Aircraft-swap disposal rule (PR #85 M1/L12/L17/L19):** every A380 form that holds a Coherent client or the def instance MUST be disposed in `SwitchAircraft`'s cleanup (MCDU, EFB, OANS, RMP, ECL checklist + the per-aircraft monitor-manager forms). A hide-on-close form (RMP) needs its teardown in `Dispose(bool)` — `Form.Dispose()` skips `OnFormClosed`, and `Close()` is cancelled by the hide guard. Capture the OUTGOING def at the top of `SwitchAircraft` (`oldAircraft`) for old-instance cleanup: `StopAllMotion()` (seat/slider ramp timers otherwise write L:vars at the new aircraft for ~8 s) and `StopA380EWDMonitor(oldAircraft)` (clears `EwdScrapeHandlesAnnounce` on the right instance). A swap TO the A380 also arms `announcer.Suppressed` (cleared in the swap grace timer) so the E/WD memo set doesn't burst-announce mid-registration.

**Landing-rate + landing-G output hotkeys (aircraft-AGNOSTIC — work on every aircraft).** `Ctrl+Shift+R` = last landing rate (`PLANE TOUCHDOWN NORMAL VELOCITY` ×60 → fpm, read live from the persistent SimVar cache — the sim latches it at touchdown), `Ctrl+Shift+G` = last landing peak g. New `Services/LandingRateAnnouncer` opens a 4 s peak-g capture window at the airborne→ground edge (`justTouchedDown` in MainForm's `SIM_ON_GROUND` handler), fed by the always-on `G FORCE` base SimVar. New base SimVars `G_FORCE` + `PLANE_TOUCHDOWN_NORMAL_VELOCITY` (Continuous, IsAnnounced=false) in `BaseAircraftDefinition.GetBaseVariables`. Both hotkeys say "No landing recorded this session" before any landing. (Output-mode chords; each mode has its own keyset so they don't collide with the input-mode Ctrl+Shift+R RMP / output-mode R-TCAS.)

**Unified Cockpit panel.** The former separate "Cockpit Door", "Windows and Shades" and "Cockpit" pedestal panels are merged into ONE organized `p["Cockpit"]` (door + door-video → sliding windows → shades/visors → openable panels → seats/armrests); door video pulled out of Recorder and Misc; `d["Cockpit"]` carries Cabin Ready. Brake-values check: verified live the brake temps/pressures read real values (temp 25.7 °C, accumulator 5250 psi, normal-brake 0 unbraked) and the Autobrake panel re-requests them on every open (`RequestPanelVariables`) — they update when given.

**Crew SEATS are 8 toggle BUTTONS (press to start, press again to stop + speak position) — 2026-06, user request, supersedes BOTH the b065970 "ramp the slider" AND the intermediate 3-state-combo motor design.** Two earlier bugs drove this: (1) the "just a tick, no sustained motor sound" — the seat motor audio (`sound.xml` `seatmotor{fwd,back,up,down}`) is a Wwise **`Continuous` loop gated by a `Derived="true"` RTPC = the per-frame DERIVATIVE of the position L:var** (`SEAT_{CPT,FO}_MOVE_{UP_DOWN,FWD_AFT}`, 0–100); a write must change the var EVERY frame or the loop only plays its onset then fades (`FadeOutTime=0.1`). (2) the combo "start/stop/start + spurious down/up 5%" — MainForm periodically re-reads a combo's backing var; the synthetic motor var reads 0 → snaps the combo to "Stopped" → re-fires `HandleUIVariableSet` → restart + bogus announce. **Fix = `RenderAsButton` toggle buttons** (MainForm fires `HandleUIVariableSet(varKey, 1, …)` on the click edge only, no periodic re-read, so the snap-back can't happen). Eight buttons `SEATBTN_{CPT,FO}_{UP,DOWN,FWD,AFT}` (`SeatBtn` helper) + four read-only position vars `SEAT_{CPT,FO}_MOVE_{UP_DOWN,FWD_AFT}` (`SeatPos`). `_seatButtonMap` maps each button → `(PosVar, Dir ±1)`; the HandleUIVariableSet branch calls `ToggleSeatMotor`: if that axis is already moving this dir → stop + `AnnounceSeatPosition` (+ `RequestVariable` forceUpdate); else seed `_seatMotorPos` from the cache and start a **20 ms** UI-thread `SeatMotorTick` firing a UNIQUE clamped read-modify-write via the calc path `<seq> 0 * (L:VAR) 0.4 + 100 min (>L:VAR)` (up) / `0.4 - 0 max` (down) — the `<seq> 0 *` prefix makes each calc string unique so MobiFlight doesn't DEDUP it (identical strings are registered+fired once; that dedup was the *real* "tick once" cause), and the per-frame change keeps the derivative non-zero → sustained motor noise. **Position read-out on stop** speaks a BAND not a percentage: `SeatBand` → fully up/up/slightly up/mid travel/slightly down/down/fully down (+ "{pct} percent"); `TryGetDisplayOverride` renders the 4 position vars the same way. 8 s safety cap stops a forgotten-moving axis; at the 0/100 clamp the writes no-op and the loop fades on its own. **Direction labels (Up=+var / Forward=+var) NOT visually confirmed** — if a seat moves the wrong way, swap the Dir sign in `_seatButtonMap` (trivial). **Armrests / sunshades / visors KEEP the `RampSliderTo` slider** — no motor sound in `sound.xml`, so a position target is the right model there.

**A32NX PRESS SD page fix.** The plain `A32NX_PRESS_CABIN_ALTITUDE` / `_CABIN_VS` / `_CABIN_DELTA_PRESSURE` names DO NOT EXIST on the A32NX (read static 0) — the A32NX publishes cab-press via the CPC ARINC429 words `A32NX_PRESS_CPC_1_CABIN_ALTITUDE` / `_CABIN_VS` / `_CABIN_DELTA_PRESSURE` / `_OUTFLOW_VALVE_OPEN_PERCENTAGE` (decoded, "not available" when the SSM is invalid). Fixed.

**Button rule clarified (2026-06 audit): only TRUE one-shot momentary actions are buttons; any on/off or multi-state control is a COMBO** (so the value is always visible/correct and a second press isn't a no-op). A button that toggles a hidden state and never updates its label is the bug to avoid — e.g. the A32NX APU Start PB was a `RenderAsButton` toggle whose label never changed → reverted to a combo. The A380 Fire Test + Cargo Smoke Detection Test were likewise reverted to Off/On combos. Buttons that REMAIN: the ECAM-CP keys, chronometer Start-Stop/Reset, cabin/mechanic calls, ATC ack (all momentary pulses). If a button must show state, set `StateVariable` (the 0/1 indicator L:var) so MainForm updates its label on each press (the Fenix pattern). The unused `ToggleBtn` helper was removed.

**Ground/external power kept next to the battery controls** in the ELEC panel (user request): A380 `p["ELEC"]` moves the 4 `EXT_PWR_*_PB_IS_ON` right after the 4 battery PBs; the A32NX already had EXT PWR adjacent to the 2 batteries.

**ARINC bit-packed discrete words DECODED (no longer deferred), both aircraft.** A `Bit(bit, set, clr, invert)` helper (A380SdRows) decodes a 1-based SSM-gated bit of an ARINC discrete word. A380 COND: cabin fans enabled + fan 1-4 faults (VCS word bits 17/18-21), fwd/bulk cargo extract fans (13/15), fwd/bulk cargo isolation valves (14/16), hot-air 1/2 valves (TCS 15/16), pack 1/2 operative (AGS 13/14); BLEED: per-pack-valve flow (`A32NX_PNEU_PACK_n_FLOW_VALVE_m_FLOW_RATE` 0..1 -> %) + pack operative. A32NX COND: hot-air valve (ACSC word 1 bit 20, **inverted** — open = bit clear), hot-air switch (23), cabin fan 1/2 fault (25/26), trim-air valve positions; BLEED: HP valve, RAM AIR, pack 1/2 flow (`A32NX_COND_PACK_FLOW_n` %).

**Engine page "values don't change" = the SD box is a SNAPSHOT, not a wrong var.** Verified live on the A380: `A32NX_ENGINE_N1:1` tracked 18.9% (idle) -> 76.5% (full throttle). The SD/ECAM-CP status box is OnRequest — it updates on page-select / F5, not continuously. (Possible enhancement: auto-refresh the SD box while open.) **A32NX engine-page LIVE check is DEFERRED until loaded into the A32NX** — verify `A32NX_ENGINE_N1:1/2` etc. track with throttle and that the SD Engine page reads them; same snapshot behaviour expected.

**DOCUMENTED FOLLOW-UPS (exact var lists in the session agent reports — execute mechanically when loaded into the A32NX):** (1) A32NX ECAM-CP HVar buttons already fire as momentary buttons via `SendButtonPressRelease` (no change needed; cosmetic-only if unifying with the A380 style). (2) A32NX SD completeness: ELEC (TR 1/2/ESS V+A, gen 1/2 freq, bat 1/2 current, EXT PWR V+Hz, STAT INV V+Hz, IDG temps), FUEL (5 per-tank quantities + crossfeed), WHEEL (gear down-lock per leg via `A32NX_LGCIU_{1,2}_DISCRETE_WORD_1/3`, anti-skid), APU (bleed pressure, gen freq), HYD (reservoir low/air-press/OVHT, pump PB state, e-pump OVHT). (3) A32NX decoded upper-E/WD path (thrust mode + N1/EGT/N2/FF/FOB + SFCC flap config) — currently scrape-only. (4) A32NX panel adds: RMP NAV button, GPU-available readout, rain repellent, RAT manual deploy, integral/standby-compass lights, ELEC GALLEY.

**Every other A380 cockpit control is a COMBO BOX (selectors; buttons only for the ECAM-CP/test set above and the FCU push/pull).** Standardised for consistent screen-reader navigation: Sel/OnOff/OffAuto/Press all render combos (the `Sel` helper forces `RenderAsButton=false`; the `button:` param is ignored). The previously button-rendered `Evt` controls were converted:
- Engine MASTER 1-4 and the 4 CROSSFEED valves → one Off/On (Closed/Open) combo each, state from the stock fuel-valve SimVar, set fires `FUELSYSTEM_VALVE_OPEN/CLOSE` (ids 1-4 / 46-49).
- DOORS → **REMOVED from the A380 entirely (2026-06).** They were the root cause of the aircraft-detection break — see the "doors root-caused" note in the DEFERRED block below. External door-opens are still surfaced by the EWD "DOOR … NOT CLOSED" memo.
- JETWAY / STAIRS control combos were REMOVED — these services are operated on the flyPad Ground page, not via panels. Only a read-only `JETWAY_MOVING_STATE` (Moving/Stopped) motion readout remains; `TOGGLE_JETWAY`/`TOGGLE_RAMPTRUCK` are no longer used in the def.
- Transponder IDENT, VHF SWAP → Off/Idle action combos via the new `Act()` helper (a combo with NO real backing var whose set is fully handled in `HandleUIVariableSet`; OnRequest so a non-existent L-var isn't monitored).
**Enabler:** MainForm's SimVar-combo set path now calls `currentAircraft.HandleUIVariableSet(...)` FIRST (mirroring the LVar-combo path) — so a combo whose STATE is a SimVar but whose CONTROL is a K-event works; the A320 light cases return false and fall through unchanged. **KEPT as buttons:** the FCU/AP push-pull (`A32NX.FCU_*_PUSH/PULL`, Event type, hit the final button branch). **EDIT FIELDS:** any `_SET` key (squawk `TRANSPONDER_CODE_SET`, COM `COM_STANDBY_FREQUENCY_SET:n`, temps, manual pressurization) renders a numeric/text input via MainForm's `varKey.Contains("_SET")` branch. All conversions live-verified (engine valve 1, crossfeed 46 actuated; door controls have since been removed — see the DEFERRED door note).

### HorizonSim 787-9 CDU (Coherent debugger — the HTTP bridge was RETIRED 2026-06-19; the EFB was REMOVED 2026-06)

The WT Boeing FMC (CDU) is read AND driven over the MSFS Coherent GT remote
debugger (`http://127.0.0.1:19999`), exactly like the A380 MFD/flyPad. **There is NO HTTP bridge,
NO injected JS in the aircraft package, and NO `HS787ModPackageManager` HTML patching anymore** —
all of that (`EFBBridgeServer` :19778, `hs787-mfd-bridge.js`, `hs787-efb-bridge.js`, the FS2020
override package / FS2024 in-place patching, `HS787CommunityFolderForm`) was deleted. The user no
longer installs a Community-folder mod for the 787; nothing needs a sim restart.
